
-----title
永安（沙县） (出生地)
-----detail

class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1120')">1091-1120年</a>，1-30岁</div><div id='c3c55bf4f5f7481693aff39eef58b05d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　是年出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1096')">1092-1096年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　居乡读书，聪敏绝伦。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1099')">1098-1099年</a>　居乡读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　已能文，出语惊人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1104')">1101-1104年</a>　居乡读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　作《代人上县令》<div id='poem_1236842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人上县令书<span class='inlineComment2'>（时年十五）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236842")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236842'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236842'>某闻士人趋走王公大人之门，有为名者，有为利者，有不为名利者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236842_comment'></div>为名之士，朝夕汲汲，兀坐冥搜，一篇之出，惟恐人之不己知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236842_comment'></div>为利之士，诉穷叙德，缄封求谒，号寒啼饥，若不能朝暮者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236842_comment'></div>有不为名利者，其患难之人乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236842_comment'></div>某也无状，盖将患难之事，仰首一鸣，以期左右之见念矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236842_comment'></div>某裳如垂磬，地无置锥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236842_comment'></div>家父执役于公，以给伏腊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236842_comment'></div>而某不免寄食于村落，与十数学生相聚，少资束脯，以申反哺之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236842_comment'></div>驱驰近岁，昨日方还，双亲欣然，遂宽倚门之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236842_comment'></div>杀鸡为黍，各相劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236842_comment'></div>父轻醉，且遽然而起曰：「公有事焉，不可缓也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236842_comment'></div>遽到公庭，雁鹜以进，反以酒故，遂陷囹圄，呜呼痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236842_comment'></div>一岁之勤，将成一日之欢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236842_comment'></div>又岂知一日之欢，反作一家之祸乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236842_comment'></div>幸望先生察其终始之情，原其平生之迹，若果酣酒无赖、舞文犯法者，先生罪之，某复何言哉，但痛心疾首而已矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236842_comment'></div>若岁暮冬寒，父子忽然相睹，閤门之内把酒相劳，则其情可恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236842_comment'></div>某今日伏拜庭下，幸先生垂骨肉之恩，故虽殒灭，亦不足为先生报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236842_comment'></div>忧惧之深，言不成章，俟罪而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1236842_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　居乡读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1110')">1107-1110年</a>　居乡求学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年7月</a>　游陈渊之门，有上杨时书，欲拜识之。作品：《上龟山先生杨博士》<div id='poem_1236840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上龟山先生杨博士书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236840")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236840'>乡侄邓某谨裁书上提宫博士先生阁下：嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236840_comment'></div>世人学者急于爵禄之奉，缀缉腐语以追时好，凡不可以取青紫者，无复给视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236840_comment'></div>穷年兀兀，老死章句，识者悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236840_comment'></div>至于卓荦瑰奇之士，未始数数于此者，则必箕踞高吟，游心景物，收拾天地精英，以实锦囊，直鄙时辈为嘈嘈蝇蚋，若不可与之言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236840_comment'></div>殆不知画饼象龙，均于无用，又乌可以五十步笑百步哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236840_comment'></div>幸而有知读圣人之书，而求其所以言者，不得于经则必求于世儒之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236840_comment'></div>即世儒之说而求之，其亲见异闻，往往出人意表，恍惚变化，不可捕捉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236840_comment'></div>凡所言者皆人之所不可言，凡所行者皆人之所不可行，悉心竭力，莫知所归，则又将去而之佛、老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236840_comment'></div>呜呼，道之不明，真学者之不幸也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236840_comment'></div>某于众人不幸之中，若天与之幸者，得游于令婿知默之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236840_comment'></div>虽驽钝之质不能窥测其涯涘，然窃尝闻之，知默之言得于先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236840_comment'></div>先生之学非有瑰伟俶诡之论，乔诘卓鸷之节，以耸世俗之观听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236840_comment'></div>独于行止疾徐而知尧舜之道，于不为已甚而得孔子之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236840_comment'></div>其所言者，人皆可言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236840_comment'></div>其所行者，人皆可行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236840_comment'></div>某之心于是知所向，某之力于是知可以勉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236840_comment'></div>盖亦尝因其可言者，以思其所未能言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236840_comment'></div>因其所可行者，以思其所未能行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236840_comment'></div>时见先生卓然不可企及，向风之行，愿识之志，往往参前倚衡，如或见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236840_comment'></div>今先生去而家于毗陵，徘徊乡郡，某适在此，幸可以瞻拜屦舄，此某所以辄布区区之诚，仰干将命，初不知其才之可进与否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236840_comment'></div>昔仪封人将见孔子，曰：「君子之至于斯也，吾未尝不得见也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236840_comment'></div>古之人其乐见君子也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236840_comment'></div>然仪封人之贤否，虽不可知，而其姓字且不见于《论语》，则亦必其无大过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236840_comment'></div>某虽不肖，不足以望君子之尘，至其乐见君子之心，于仪封人若无甚愧，不识先生肯与之一见否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236840_comment'></div>干冒威严，惶惧之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1236840_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1117')">1112-1117年</a>　居乡求学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　居乡。是春，撰《论书》<div id='poem_1236886' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236886' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236886?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236886")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236886_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236886'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236886'>持笔如驭将，柔顺从指者皆非良材，而狰狞纵逸者亦不可制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236886_comment'></div>要当兴伏抑按，每从人欲，而纸上戛戛，自有生意，然后为妙笔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236886_comment'></div>近世人多作无骨字，盱睢侧媚，有乞怜之态，故其所用者皆无心冗毫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236886_comment'></div>此笔才入手，则诸葛所制当为生硬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236886_comment'></div>不能用诸葛笔而欲作字，如项羽弃范增而欲取中原也，其可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1236886'>墨以黑为体，以光为神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236886_comment'></div>神采轻浮，不能深黑，譬如纨绮子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236886_comment'></div>浓字大画，黑而无光，亦一田舍翁耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236886_comment'></div>眉山老仙谓陈瞻墨，潘生不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236886_comment'></div>瞻何为者，敢冀潘耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236886_comment'></div>此论未公，吾不凭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1236886'>研不必甚佳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236886_comment'></div>比尝见士人相矜曰：此端也，其色莹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236886_comment'></div>彼歙也，其文致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236886_comment'></div>不知文与色亦何与于墨乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236886_comment'></div>皆好奇之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236886_comment'></div>大抵石在山者燥、在水者脆，脆者不能以制墨，而燥者又不行笔，二者胥失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236886_comment'></div>去是二病，虽凤咮足矣，亦何必近舍皇甫湜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1236886'>张长史脱帽露顶，抵掌于八仙之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236886_comment'></div>今物化数百年矣，每观其字，则恍然逸韵，犹在目前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236886_comment'></div>颜鲁公作字端严可畏，张之屋壁，奸人胆落，与长史无毫发相类，而史氏谓鲁公独传其法，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236886_comment'></div>盖字法三昧，当以神悟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236886_comment'></div>既悟矣，如嗣宗老宿，或以棒，或以喝，或作老婆态，种种不等，要之皆西来意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1236886'>本朝评书，以君谟为第一，信嘉祐之间可以魁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236886_comment'></div>苏、黄继出，文妙天下，而书又能张其军，于君谟若无甚愧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236886_comment'></div>然君谟如杜甫诗，无一字无来处，纵横上下，皆藏古意，学之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236886_comment'></div>苏、黄资质过人，笔力天出，其太白诗乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236886_comment'></div>深得其趣者，自当见其优劣矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1236886'>米芾，楚狂者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236886_comment'></div>作字清远，有晋、宋气，所恨者但能行书耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236886_comment'></div>真如立，行如行，草如走，三者不可阙一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236886_comment'></div>若用《春秋》之法责备贤者，则米芾在所惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236886_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1236886'>丹霞赜师学余书未半年，亦有可观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236886_comment'></div>今来求益，吾术穷矣，姑使之择笔墨之精者以利其器，然后品藻古今能字者，以俾其自取耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236886_comment'></div>赜勉之，风韵不凡，他日所学当有不止于书者，吾将并得而告也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236886_comment'></div>政和戊戌春，栟榈邓肃朝阳堂书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1236886_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1119')">1118-1119年</a>　丁父忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年2月</a>　居乡丁忧。二月，结识李纲，为忘年交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　初春，有诗与李纲唱和。作品：《寒梅上李舍人诗》<div id='poem_76697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寒梅上李舍人</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76697")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76697'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76697'>穷山触目纷茅苇，此意昏昏谁可洗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76697'>竹间忽<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗集作横）</span>破一枝梅，对月嫣然耿寒水。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76697'>吟诗索酒满高堂，穿帘的皪射晶光。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76697'>世上膻荤来不到，剪剪天风吹冷香。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76697'>人言百花睡未起，独冠群芳差可喜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76697'>那知和羹自有期，未用<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗集作行事）</span>争雄压桃李。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76697'>但怜雨雪正濛濛，寒意未舒万象穷。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76697'>故作选锋驱残腊，挽回天地变春风。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76697'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_76697_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　请李纲为其所藏画题跋，李纲为作《墨戏六首》。二人反复唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　与李纲同游陈氏园。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　仲春，有和李纲春雪诗。作品：《和李梁溪春雪韵二首》<div id='poem_76533' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76533' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76533?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和李梁溪春雪韵二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76533")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76533_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76533'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76533'>白白朱朱春已深，那知雪意更阴阴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76533_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76533'>落花几阵遮山密，穿褐馀寒赖酒禁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76533_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76533'>骑马不前真有恨，留衣过腊岂无心。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76533_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76533'>等为迁客俱逢雪，谁似梁溪独醉吟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76533_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76533'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76533_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76532' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76532' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76532?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76532_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76532'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76532'>玄冥忽欲作春容，不许东君利自封。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76532'>已使素英拖暖絮，更摧妖艳别寒松。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76532'>那知往事思飞燕，预庆丰年免象龙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76532'>向有谪仙诗句好，何妨闭户醉金钟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76532_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76532'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76532_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　与李纲唱和荼蘼、岩桂、芍药诸诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　与李纲同游栖云寺，有唱和诗并跋文。作品：《跋罗右文李左史题栖云真戒大师营治》<div id='poem_1236875' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236875' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236875?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋罗右文李左史题栖云真戒大师营治</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236875")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236875_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236875'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236875'>沙县佛宫殆以百计，独无轮藏以耸观者，栖云禅院真戒大师可臣首造之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236875_comment'></div>金碧相照，恍若天宫，盖闽中所未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236875_comment'></div>又以谓传公之建藏，三藏之传经，皆唱吾道者，因架阁以报之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236875_comment'></div>又立堂于殿下，以招具眼人同观藏教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236875_comment'></div>白石清泉之间，明窗净几，如在世外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236875_comment'></div>右文罗公见曰：「此老当为吾邦之杰然者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236875_comment'></div>叹赏久之，乃纪以诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236875_comment'></div>而左史李公亦曰：「岂特此邦耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236875_comment'></div>虽求之天下，指不多屈」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236875_comment'></div>遂次其韵，亦以赠焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236875_comment'></div>且二公平日为吾道主盟，近年以来，义不辱于金、张、贾、马之门，宁居冷宦，聊以卒岁耳，决非假人以言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236875_comment'></div>孟子曰：「观远臣以其所主，观近臣以其所为主」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236875_comment'></div>不知真戒者，但观其所主，则其人可知矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1236875_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　与李纲唱和。作品：《次韵李舍人》<div id='poem_76598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵李舍人</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76598")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76598'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76598'>道山文章伯，杖履作幽栖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76598'>笔砚为戏事，业落翻墨螭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76598'>平生百万言，定相初不离。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76598'>更怜世间士，尘网深相闱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76598'>笑踵双林辙，誓破万夫疑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76598'>八面列神王，剑戟森携持。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76598'>怒目干龙宫，机缄绝谋惟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76598'>佛语浩无际，天地如可弥。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76598'>笑谈一转毕，璿玑时未移。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76598'>见者皆了了，钝根化神机。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76598'>不然分三藏，谁能俱不遗。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76598'>白头钻故纸，底是出头时。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76598'>此恩今欲报，四顾将谁依。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76598'>在佛本无说，于公亦何为。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76598'>珍重谪仙人，登山力未疲。<div id='poem_sentence_14_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_76598'>天涯渺万里，著处即为归。<div id='poem_sentence_15_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_76598'>随缘作赞叹，妙语何奇奇。<div id='poem_sentence_16_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_76598'>置之天壤间，千古无敢非。<div id='poem_sentence_17_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_76598'>我生多肉障，烦公示宝篦。<div id='poem_sentence_18_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_76598'>请作一言蔽，牟尼即仲尼。<div id='poem_sentence_19_76598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_76598'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_76598_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年4月15日</a>　跋李纲《放鲎文》作品：《跋李舍人放鲎文》<div id='poem_1236869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236869' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236869?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋李舍人放鲎文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年4月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236869")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236869_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236869'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236869'>夏四月己卯，侍舍人李公游于隐圃，公以放鲎之事语某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236869_comment'></div>闻而异之，乃请曰：「幸先生书焉，以为众生福田」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236869_comment'></div>公不可，曰：「梦寐之事，未暇也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236869_comment'></div>明日造门，复请曰：「南海之民恃鱼为命，残鲎而食者岁以万计，未闻有以梦告者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236869_comment'></div>今独于先生而祈焉，不书之，何以耸见闻而助教化」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236869_comment'></div>公乃恻焉，为之挥毫，叙其残杀之害为甚酷，考其口腹之适为甚微，使见之者皆若亲感其梦，而视血气之类皆为鲎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236869_comment'></div>则凡有恻隐之心者，其谁忍杀之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236869_comment'></div>爱物之仁，固不可量数，又岂止一鲎而已耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236869_comment'></div>昔人尝谓螺蚌蚬蛤之类，赋性不全，杀之无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236869_comment'></div>苏子有言：此乃懦陋顽固众生不能自诉报怨者，若杀之，正是欺善怕恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236869_comment'></div>夫鲎之为物，介重迟，潜逃深渺，岂亦赋性不足者之类乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236869_comment'></div>今且能感梦如此，则又乌知其不能自诉耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236869_comment'></div>是亦可畏哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236869_comment'></div>此某所以请公之书而愿为刊之，且道其所念，以告观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236869_comment'></div>受五日，门人邓某。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1236869_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年4月</a>　初夏，送菖蒲、竹笋与李纲，李纲有诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年4月</a>　有诗送丹霞禅院的宗本禅师。作品：《送丹霞》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年4月</a>　有诗与丹霞禅院的宗本禅师唱和交往。作品：《访丹霞》《谢丹霞老师》<div id='poem_76608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>访丹霞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76608")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76608'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76608'>烟云著天无寸空，寒窗瑟瑟夜号风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76608'>浩歌出门何所诣，故人飞锡梵王宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76608'>扣门兀坐寂无语，衲破蒙头面如土。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76608'>逢场聊复触机锋，千偈澜翻疾风雨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76608'>我生鼻孔自撩天，笑将龙肉比谈禅。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76608'>针水相投得吾子，帖肉汗衫今脱然。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76608'>但怜净业犹诗酒，醉笔时作蛟龙走。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76608'>傥惟语默两无妨，凭公刻烛联千首。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76608'>况是雪意政相留，慎勿匆匆抚刀头。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76608'>明日谈笑作春色，同在琼瑶十二楼。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76608'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_76608_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢丹霞老师</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76702")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76702'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76702'>丹霞脩何行，天花雨红英。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76702'>草莽化金碧，宴坐十年成。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76702'>落笔多奇语，酬唱皆名卿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76702'>微言寄祸福，无心天籁鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76702'>顷年来七峰，见我眼增明。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76702'>西来的的意，一语贯三乘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76702'>坐令尘土人，弹指悟无生。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76702'>别来今许久，夜梦飞爽灵。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76702'>新诗忽入手，春风死草萌。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76702'>公以慧生定，我自明而诚。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76702'>相望虽千里，秋风共一清。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76702'>去去勿作念，明鉴无将迎。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76702'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_76702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年5月</a>　仲夏五月，邓肃家枯梅产芝，李纲有诗赋咏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年6月18日</a>　同李纲聚会凝翠阁，游泛碧斋，有诗唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年7月19日</a>　于乃父坟旁筑室，李纲题名曰“显亲”。志宏有诗谢之。作品：《谢李舍人题额》<div id='poem_76705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢李舍人题额</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年7月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76705")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76705'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76705'>寸草春未报，秋风树不停。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76705'>三年真忽尔，过隙白驹奔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76705'>庐坟吾岂敢，北堂有老人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76705'>作庵居释子，佛事勤朝昏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76705'>太史怜此意，高额揭显亲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76705'>梁间垂玉箸，壁上霭飞云。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76705'>顾我何为者，传家空一经。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76705'>栖迟已三十，寒灯尚短檠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76705'>北辕将适楚，捩手或翻羹。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76705'>那能为亲显，只可充添丁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76705'>但念我先人，白首困飘零。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76705'>射策不逢赏，青衫脱王庭。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76705'>今焉逢太史，发挥身后名。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76705'>坐令九泉下，冷骨复生春。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76705'>显扬政在此，松楸万世荣。<div id='poem_sentence_14_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_76705'>作诗敢论报，欲为肌上铭。<div id='poem_sentence_15_76705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_76705'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_76705_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年7月</a>　李纲有诗题显亲庵，邓肃又和作。作品：《题显亲庵谨次严韵》<div id='poem_76719' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76719' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76719?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题显亲庵谨次严韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76719")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76719_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76719'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76719'>寒芦败苇秋风严，魏紫姚黄春色妍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76719'>谁能不随天地转，开阖自我古无前。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76719'>秋花忽从三月盛，引得好诗来相庆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76719'>为见漫空儿女姿，义气稍回君子正。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76719'>我顷失鱼缘钩直，抱璞未酬不须泣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76719'>天生我辈岂偶然，但驱百怪归篇什。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76719'>惭愧梅仙情最亲，期我看花三省身。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76719'>已趁春风聊一笑，更仿<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑当作傲）</span>秋霜不改春。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76719'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_76719_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年7月</a>　题诗陈公叙舫斋，与李纲唱和。作品：《舫斋》<div id='poem_76685' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76685' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76685?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舫斋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76685")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76685_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76685'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76685'>寓形天宇间，一枝慎所处。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76685'>到眼无溪山，堆胸自尘土。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76685'>陈子作舫斋，端能世外趣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76685'>笑傲风波境，恬无风波虑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76685'>循本鱼可观，灰心鸥自舞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76685'>风景虽可人，公乎聊四顾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76685'>纷纷逐末流，谁援沉迷苦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76685'>吾事在济川，慎勿五湖去。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76685_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76685'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_76685_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年8月</a>　中秋前后，与李纲唱和岩桂诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年9月15日</a>　九月十五日夜，与李纲、陈兴宗登阁观月、乘船泛溪，有诗词唱和。作品：《凝翠阁陪李梁溪次韵》《陪李梁溪游泛碧》《一剪梅•题泛碧斋》<div id='poem_76562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>凝翠阁陪李梁溪次韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年9月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76562")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76562'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76562'>栏前碧玉四围宽，满座清风文字欢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76562'>霜气袭人秋更爽，溪光耿月夜生寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76562'>登临顾我那能赋，姓字从公遂不漫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76562'>此景此时难再得，相思但把锦囊看。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76562'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76562_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陪李梁溪游泛碧</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年9月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76686")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76686'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76686'>凉天夜无云，寒江秋更碧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76686'>冷照月华中，水天同一色。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76686'>画船渺中流，三更群动寂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76686'>清风远相随，芦花秋瑟瑟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76686'>近山得桂香，隔烟起渔笛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76686'>楼台半有无，疑是化人国。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76686'>我生本无事，钓竿勤水石。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76686'>今宵更可人，仍侍君子侧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76686'>浪登元礼舟，本非谪仙敌。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76686'>敛手看挥毫，光芒腾万尺。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76686'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_76686_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>一剪梅 题泛碧斋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年9月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76728")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76728'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76728'>雨过春山翠欲浮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76728'>影落寒溪碧玉流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76728'>片帆乘兴挂东风，夹岸花香拥去舟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76728'>樽酒时追李郭游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76728'>醉卧烟波万事休。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76728'>梦回风定斗杓寒，渔笛一声天地秋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_76728_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年9月28日</a>　九月二十八日，陈渊为文祭志宏父南夫。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2c0f9ba5901944b894736ab13cf6b1e6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2c0f9ba5901944b894736ab13cf6b1e6");'><span id='2c0f9ba5901944b894736ab13cf6b1e6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>，31岁</div><div id='2c0f9ba5901944b894736ab13cf6b1e6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年3月</a>　居乡，上书刘韐献平方腊之策。作品：《上刘延康》<div id='poem_1236841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上刘延康书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236841")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236841'>某月某日，南剑州上舍贡士邓某谨斋戒沐浴，裁书东拜，寓献判府经略大学相府先生钧席：某尝读颜真卿、杲卿及张巡、许远四公列传，见其为唐社稷奋身不顾，守节死义，名高日月，未尝不拊髀而叹曰：嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236841_comment'></div>天地英杰之气，勃郁未吐，不知几千百年乃钟若人，以为万世标准，是其可多得哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236841_comment'></div>故天下之人有胁肩谄笑能容悦者，亦不敢借此数公，以谀今之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236841_comment'></div>虽好大喜功，不计能否，欲追配古人者，闻此数公，亦必悚然起，惕然惧，歉然而不敢当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236841_comment'></div>呜呼，是果不敢当乎，抑有待而后传乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236841_comment'></div>天地英杰之气，亦安知其不再吐耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236841_comment'></div>今年睦、歙寇啸山谷，奋臂疾呼，而群小附之，攻城围邑，江浙骚然，官吏狼顾，丧魂沮魄，弃城而遁者不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236841_comment'></div>会稽大府，又贼所必争之地，奔命来寇，动以千计，中外闻之，莫不为之股慄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236841_comment'></div>而判府大学报国赤心，可动天地，驱兵力战，卒保城池，使贼众累然卵破草折，是可谓障百川而东之，回狂澜于既倒者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236841_comment'></div>其视大唐四公，又不知孰为优劣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236841_comment'></div>虽然，平原日窘，真卿弃之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236841_comment'></div>常山力竭，杲卿死之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236841_comment'></div>睢阳之救不至，张巡、许远亦连颈就戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236841_comment'></div>夫真卿之去，虽出于不得已，要非功成而名遂者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236841_comment'></div>三公死节，虽人所难，然身可死也，其于民社之寄，无乃误所委乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236841_comment'></div>故以功烈论之，则四公犹有所愧，独于先生一无疵焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236841_comment'></div>盖节义等于四公，而勋又远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236841_comment'></div>呜呼，至矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236841_comment'></div>其不可企及哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236841_comment'></div>此非特某之私言也，乃天下之公论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236841_comment'></div>亦非特天下之公论也，顾虽如先生谦冲退托，亦不能自谓其不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236841_comment'></div>以今之人慕彼四公且勤若此，至不知天下之人企望先生之盛德，复何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236841_comment'></div>某虽无似，其生得与先生同时，且家于闽中，而喜于从学，又获与令弟为齑盐之友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236841_comment'></div>家于闽中，是邻先生之居也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236841_comment'></div>喜于从学，是习先生之业也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236841_comment'></div>复与令弟为友，是其姓字可以达于左右者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236841_comment'></div>其天幸如此，顾虽家有老母，不能远去扫门执鞭，以快平生之愿，而挥毫染翰，写此精诚，亦安得独后于众人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236841_comment'></div>虽然，亦僭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236841_comment'></div>以一介贱士而干万世之功臣，贵贱贤否不啻霄壤，其率尔之罪，固亦不胜诛，亦何恃而敢为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236841_comment'></div>盖先生既立已然之功，必建未然之策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236841_comment'></div>虽奇谋妙算已定胸中，而刍荛之言或有可采者，此某所以愿有献也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236841_comment'></div>某无他能，解颇通古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236841_comment'></div>曩闻盗贼之兴，私窃念某既治其已甚，又欲阻其方来，故仰求缙绅先生之论，俯采匹夫匹妇之言，考诸古而不违，质诸今而可用，研精极虑，得十策焉，欲进九重，恨无因也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236841_comment'></div>效死有志，穷鳞可惜，谨写之别卷，以干台视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236841_comment'></div>伏幸先生留顷刻之暇，聊赐一观，或无甚谬、有可用者，惟先生委曲而审处之，非某敢自择也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236841_comment'></div>昔者有为浙东观察使者张籍，相距于五千里外，辄以书寓达，而不以僭易为嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236841_comment'></div>得非学者所为，大小君子当有以恕之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236841_comment'></div>又况籍盲于目，既为废人矣，且不能遣语，而托韩愈代之，又其区区所以自叙者，亦不过钱财以济于药耳，是皆所无足取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236841_comment'></div>某虽晚进，不足比数于人，然论才与志，则非籍比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236841_comment'></div>倘使今日得出甄陶之下，而不与草木同腐，则竭力自效，亦必不至为阁下辱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236841_comment'></div>区区毫楮，岂能既此心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236841_comment'></div>干冒钧重，不胜惶恐慄战之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1236841_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年8月15日</a>　中秋，作《丹霞清泚轩记》<div id='poem_1236896' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236896' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236896?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丹霞清泚轩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和三年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236896")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236896_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236896'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236896'>邵武丹霞僧明赜作轩于其院之西，中植菖蒲数种，郁然几案间，不远数百里，来乞名于栟榈邓某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236896_comment'></div>某名曰清泚轩，盖取东坡赞语所谓「清且泚」是也，因为之言曰：洛阳之花，隋堤之柳，筼筜之竹，徂徕之松，奇质老干，非不可喜，要之必资粪壤，乃克有生，是以未能脱然仙去，不离尘土间物耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236896_comment'></div>独菖蒲之生不事此，粲粲怪石，涓涓清泉，泉石相映，凛生寒风，于此苍然得意，四时一色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236896_comment'></div>顾其与凡草木同列哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236896_comment'></div>其节如夷、齐之高，其韵如嵇、阮之胜，其清绝如子猷之泛雪，其脱洒如列子之御风，其谢宠辱如扁舟之范蠡，其安淡泊如钓台之子陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236896_comment'></div>呜呼，至哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236896_comment'></div>非胸中有是德者，乌能嗜此物哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236896_comment'></div>东坡先生首唱此风，且为赞叙以问安否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236896_comment'></div>彼能轻死生，傲爵禄，高视四海，若无介意者，独于此切切，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236896_comment'></div>盖公所嗜之意不在菖蒲，直寄焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236896_comment'></div>赜能为东坡之意乎，明窗净几，坐见古人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236896_comment'></div>如其不然，则所嗜一草芥而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236896_comment'></div>赜作字吟诗，有吾党风格，其种菖蒲而喜之，意决有在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236896_comment'></div>虽然，愿师进之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236896_comment'></div>法眼有云：「倏然纤芥在，此岸永淹留」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236896_comment'></div>师其无留焉可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236896_comment'></div>宣和辛丑中秋，瑞芝轩书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1236896_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年10月</a>　冬，作《和谢吏部铁字韵三十四首》，陈渊有唱和。<div id='poem_76644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和谢吏部铁字韵三十四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76644")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76644'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76644'>切切寒虫常在耳，未识词源万斛水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76644'>忽开玉轴见奇文，光怪摩空乱眸子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76644'>太傅江左风流人，灵运在家元不嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76644'>家世千年今复振，落笔飘飘语更真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76644'>顿足忘言惊妙绝，欲续貂蝉恨才拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76644'>铅刀那敢望神剑，舒屈无方岂常铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76644'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76644_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76643?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76643'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76643'>穷居如将豆塞耳，一泓自足牛蹄水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76643'>那知邻境有人豪，笑观造化但儿子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76643'>笔端万字惊倒人，春色秋风随喜嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76643'>一读锦囊殆仙去，欲借云軿遂朝真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76643'>更当负笈慰愁绝，凭公一扫平生拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76643'>门人益亲自得回，会观踏破门限铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76643'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76643_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76642?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76642'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76642'>世上区区蝇狗耳，不复解缨濯清水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76642'>只知贪雀不留珠，可怜认贼翻为子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76642'>珍重谢公天下人，冷居林泉曾不嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76642'>云烟万木观不足，却把新诗为写真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76642'>高节凌云亦奇绝，不绾六印未为拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76642'>何妨笑学杜陵翁，只有布衾冷似铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76642'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76642_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76641' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76641' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76641?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76641'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76641'>仕途例皆谄笑耳，随盘方圆无定水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76641'>前年天子思奇才，霜台曾擢古君子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76641'>泛观中外傥非人，发上冲冠聊一嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76641'>那顾城狐并社鼠，好恶无私喜怒真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76641'>底事年来迹又绝，笑遁林泉似藏拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76641'>凭谁去斩佞臣头，请公速铸楚山铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76641'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76641_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76640' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76640' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76640?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76640_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76640'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76640'>四海纷纷筝笛耳，谁识子期志流水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76640'>韵高调古自难酬，得意政须副墨子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76640'>我公声价第一人，积薪居上笑不嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76640'>但将佳句妙今古，逝<span class='inlineComment2'>（道光本作誓）</span>变雕虫返太真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76640'>孟轲尝续吾道绝，功与神禹论工拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76640'>先生今复回狂澜，岂减旌阳柱铸铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76640'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76640_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76639' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76639' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76639?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76639_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76639'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76639'>引领门墙数舍耳，剑之水源自樵水<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：公邵武人也。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76639'>裹粮问道嗟未能，参前倚衡见夫子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76639'>自笑昔为尘土人，春狂时逐卖符嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76639'>年来懒惰百事废，洗空人伪惟葆真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76639'>更馀净业磨未绝，强继弥明不知拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76639'>岂是螳螂敢当车，貘兽从来食铜铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76639'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76639_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76638' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76638' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76638?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76638_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76638'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76638'>李白尝言人有耳，不当径洗颍川水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76638'>男儿出处自有时，何须锐意楚狂子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76638'>公今无意世间人，北山有灵定不嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76638'>天子政作唐虞计，谷口那留郑子真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76638'>伫观大手称奇绝，致君却笑前贤拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76638'>坐使梯航到鬼方，来寻九州贡璆铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76638'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76638_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76637?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76637'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76637'>眼中儒生聊尔耳，仅免春闱饮墨水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76637'>可怜四海万青衿，却愧建安六七子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76637'>谁似丘侯独可人，日无千篇即怒嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76637'>腐语陈言俱扫灭，奇文秀句出天真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76637'>虎头固已称诗绝，更逢安石分工拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76637'>新诗为侯特发挥，照人之明鉴磨铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76637'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76637_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76636?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76636_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76636'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76636'>结交要在相知耳，趣向不殊水投水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76636'>请看丘侯对谢公，箭锋相契无多子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76636'>丘侯平日论律人，详及谢公喜与嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76636'>一得新诗即传借，许久誇谈今见真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76636'>车马争看纷不绝，新诗那简茅檐拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76636'>脱腕供人嗟未能，安得毕升二板铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76636'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76636_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76635' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76635' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76635?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76635_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76635'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76635'>三吴恶少飞绿耳，杀人如麻壅流水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76635'>馀风往往到七闽，鱼烂鸟惊父离子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76635'>纷然回顾作流人，我侯正色聊一嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76635'>坐使仓黄万老弱，复歌太平养性真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76635'>百弊纷纷俱杜绝，四境无虞安朴拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76635'>方信哲夫自成城，不须十仞坚削铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76635'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76635_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76634?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span>纪德十一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76634'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76634'>忘心政须曲糵耳，醉仙如吸百川水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76634'>男儿不复问圣贤，杯酒力辞真竖子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76634'>我侯度量压千人，不满金钟却怒嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76634'>酒酣那复迷朱碧，苗莠犹分伪与真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76634'>人言狂药要须绝，恐溃肺肠语亦拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76634'>那知真气不可侵，乌府如今肝是铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76634'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76634_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和谢吏部铁字韵三十四首 邑官有和者亦以诗寄之其人自云御方寇有功</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76653")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76653'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76653'>寂寞相如四壁耳，陋巷萧然穷饮水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76653'>虽似退之厌权门，时作封人慕君子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76653'>惭愧知音个中人，近前不学丞相嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76653'>掀髯抵掌论今古，肺腑恢然笑语真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76653'>顷余学问非三绝，操瑟干齐谋更拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76653'>栖迟何以酬己知，吾道不移砚铸铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76653'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76653_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和谢吏部铁字韵三十四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>丘宰生日二首</a><span id='poem_sentence_1_76631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76631'>已剥群阴驱小人，四海熙熙语复嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76631'>因辟金关谪太白，不许天庭久练真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76631'>太白尘缘固未绝，肯将天巧形世拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76631'>会施霖雨满人间，归对千年忘恙铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76631'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76631_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_76630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76630'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76630'>阳复朋来七日耳，黎明当动有泉水<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76630'>阴阴寒谷未生春，天闵斯民如赤子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76630'>遂因天下生奇人，俾歌襦裤无怨嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76630'>朅来割鸡多暇日，逸韵飘飘腾九真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76630'>琼室瑶池津不绝，冷笑人间卫生拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76630'>三窃蟠桃颜益童，那复虬髯面如铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76630'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_76630'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_76630_0'>⑴ 自注：冬至后十日泉水动，此以宣和辛丑历推之耳</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_76630_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_76654' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76654' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76654?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和谢吏部铁字韵三十四首 和谢吏部</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_76654'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76654'>昔年怨声常满耳，纷纷女巫未沉水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76654'>天教我侯慰远人，坐令盗贼化君子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76654'>期年仁政遍人人，抚之如子不须嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76654'>吏民欲欺亦不忍，出言洞见胸中真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76654'>要图书问久已绝，人皆巧中渠宁拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76654'>优游黄卷有馀欢，此志不回端截铁。<div 道光本校：一作述</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76647'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76647'>瑟瑟霜风夜聒耳，小院枕衾如泼水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76647'>夜清火冷不成眠，起就短檠阅诸子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76647'>掩卷嗟嗟今古人，遗风可喜仍<span class='inlineComment2'>（道光本作亦）</span>可嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76647'>风日相怜纷无已，一笑玄之妄亦真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76647'>我今是非两俱绝，百巧百中不如拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76647'>寂然无复一念邪，那有黄冠下鞭铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76647'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76647_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76646?labeling=true' id='poem_title_76646_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_76646_0'>① 道光本校：一作述</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76646'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76646'>恶声不入伯夷耳，严陵拂袖钓寒水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76646'>古来豪杰例幽居，佩𩍚肯随舟人子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76646'>造化炉中忽为人，笑笑随缘又何嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76646'>细语粗言俱入妙，醉中不必更陶真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76646'>年来三复韦编绝，得趣无多一味拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76646'>物外翛然我已仙，不愁石髓坚如铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76646'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76646_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76645_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_76645_0'>① 道光本校：一作述</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76645'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76645'>万物纷纷一马耳，百川不同均一水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76645'>不将彼是作殊观，坐使须弥纳芥子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76645'>李白高视空无人，审言更作牙官嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76645'>可怜纸上较轻重，画饼象龙俱未真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76645'>我师宣尼四病绝，抱瓮宁作汉阴拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76645'>万变纷纷不敢侵，真室何须枢楗铁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76660'>高岩去天尺五耳，下飞瀑布千寻水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76660'>山间瘦竹映枯<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_2_76660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76660'>凡骨膻腥傥不厌，愿供薪水看脩真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76660'>高人隐几语言绝，大巧深藏端<span class='inlineComment2'>（道光本作反）</span>若拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76660'>无乃误游天目山，偶见唐公冠带铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76660'></div><div id='poem_content_76659'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76659'>人生要在行乐耳，四化相磨逝流水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76659'>溪山佳处饱遨游，莫为膻荤亲俗子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76659'>解龟谁顾谪仙人，玉局题墙亦遭嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76659'>世人例作叶公解，但喜画龙谁识真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76659'>何如便与尘寰绝，醉倒莫嫌茅店拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76659'>青骢门外系垂杨，旋乞青禾剉白铁。<div class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76658_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76658'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76658'>门前如市不入耳，忘言隐几心如水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76658'>纷华时逐长安儿，清爽何似毛锥子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76658'>我虽事业未如人，天公不等吾弗嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76658'>独步高山寻兀室，默坐烧香已悟真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76658'>世事缤纷俱谢绝，叩角自歌愚且拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76658'>谁暇投书追贾谊，更忧铜弊杂铅铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/76633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和谢吏部铁字韵三十四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>对酒二首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_76633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76633'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76633'>世上纷华蚁穴耳，东流不作西归水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76633'>号寒那用学孟郊，捉月要须追李子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76633'>一樽忽尔逢故人，高谈往往鬼神嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76633'>人间目下多忌讳，忘形惟<span class='inlineComment2'>（万历本作但）</span>有醉乡真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76633'>但得如意<span class='inlineComment2'>（道光本作渑）</span>酒不绝，四壁莫愁生事拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76633'>铸成此错吾安之，何妨与费数州铁。<div
