id='poem_sentence_0_76632'>八斗一倾聊热耳，开匣时观三尺水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76632'>指天喝月使倒行，扬波直欲斩蛟子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76632'>安得知音吾党人，相看青眼不余嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76632'>笑驱八蛮有奇策，开怀聊与话诚真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76632'>可怜吐哺风流绝，乞巧未遑姑守拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76632'>坐观明月侵虾蟆，空使玉川怀寸铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76632'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76632_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76657' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76657' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76657?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和谢吏部铁字韵三十四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>送成彦尉邵武三首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76657")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76657_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76657'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76657'>万窍于喁风割耳，梅影横斜耿烟水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76657'>杀鸡为黍政追随，七峰共作隐君子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76657'>忽举阳关饯行人，去去莫愁官长嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76657'>但知所领马曹似，清谈更觉子猷真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76657'>谷风尝讥朋友绝，子贡毋轻原宪拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76657'>期公鸿雁不空回，开缄八行划如铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76657'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76657_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76656?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>送成彦尉邵武三首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76656'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76656'>汗血神驹卓锥耳，去似苍崖决积水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76656'>据鞍年少笑西征，神仙中人梅氏子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76656'>平生胸抱不由人，点额再归曾未嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76656'>仪舌尚存斯足矣，卞玉那愁无识真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76656'>一官聊续箕裘绝，登山莫厌芒鞋拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76656'>会使狗偷扫地无，不须蜂虿挥钜铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76656'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76656_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76655' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76655?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>送成彦尉邵武三首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76655_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76655'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76655'>山头枯木半生耳，山下琉璃剪碧水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76655'>登山临水两超然，刻烛千篇对夫子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76655'>我生也是不羁人，白眼望天人共嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76655'>相逢赖有知音鲍，挥麈不疑咳唾真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76655'>子今更与竹林绝，我独凄然守株拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76655'>望公声誉腾九天，不惟去作铮铮铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76655'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76655_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76648?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和谢吏部铁字韵三十四首 别僧永肩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76648")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76648'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76648'>号寒啼饥自聒耳，火中莲花那著水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76648'>超然不复顾尘寰，空色两冥舍利子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76648'>冠巾贾岛齿平人，当时仅免退之嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76648'>何如伯升云水去，万劫不磨一点真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76648'>公今更恐情难绝，泛作飞蓬谋未拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76648'>挽袖牵裳浩不回，当知若人是真铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76648'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76648_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和谢吏部铁字韵三十四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>谢杨休三首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76663")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76663'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76663'>人生相值梗萍耳，无酒投钱亦饮水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76663'>况公家世足风流，封胡羯末又贤子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76663'>匹马来寻物外人，坐上无毡寒不嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76663'>倾盖相逢已如故，洗空机械情更真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76663'>公今在陈粮屡绝，恶圆喜方我尤拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76663'>穷愁相守两萧然，富骄何事如意铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76663'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76663_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76662' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76662' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76662?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>谢杨休三首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76662'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76662'>半夜丝簧纷养耳，舞袖香风散沉水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76662'>高堂嬉笑坐生春，不诵式微惊游子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76662'>孟公投辖虽知人，故乡千里儿曹嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76662'>毅然竟把刀头舞，百日梦归今日真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76662'>依前瘦马登高绝，未应却笑此行拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76662'>邑人脂膏子弗求，况是丘侯帽无铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76662'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76662_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76661' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76661?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>谢杨休三首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76661_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76661'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76661'>一岁无多数日耳，归心应逐东流水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76661'>遥想解鞍在于门，满室生春舞妻子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76661'>明朝去拜绛帷人，迟迟他邦冀勿嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76661'>愿及散才求入社，寓诗千里欲寻真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76661'>医门不与多病绝，无盐自献那羞拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76661'>谁知此质非良金，政须乃翁为点铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76661'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76661_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和谢吏部铁字韵三十四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>呈几叟仪曹四首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76652")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76652'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76652'>管中窥豹一斑耳，敢对江海更言水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76652'>赖公不作扬雄尾，舞雩曾许随童子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76652'>绨袍至今念故人，世人欲杀渠不嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76652'>更将妙语为高价，坐令玉表欲侔真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76652'>期公终始不相绝，回愚参鲁余亦拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76652'>异时报德但脩身，那用张良袖中铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76652'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76652_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76651?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>呈几叟仪曹四首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76651'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76651'>世上乞怜帖双耳，得失毫芒汗流水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76651'>辕驹厕鼠端可怜，笑杀物外奇男子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76651'>先生眼中无可人，将军污足渠亦嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76651'>傥欲眠时遣客去，两忘物我渊明真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76651'>世间势位日悬绝，不能变渠平日拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76651'>政如强弓五十步，无力可贯青唐铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76651'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76651_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76650?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>呈几叟仪曹四首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76650'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76650'>岭云<span class='inlineComment2'>（道光本作外）</span>去天一握耳，取死一分山下水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76650'>不辞舟车千里来，赖有陈蕃知孺子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76650'>当堂得酒觞故人，醉倒花前夜不嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76650'>我来一见欣如故，险语聊摅肺腑真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76650'>安得眼边万事绝，与君千首较工拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76650'>乐死初无锸自随，那学祠东墓费铁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76650'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76650_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76649?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76649'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76649'>忽忽百年石火耳，偃鼠不踰一腹水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76649'>胡椒百斛何为哉，箪瓢便可安颜子。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76649'>君看世间容悦人，胁肩摇尾恐人嗔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76649'>所得仅能毛发许，抵掌无由一笑真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76649'>期公便与此曹绝，折脚铛中归养拙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76649'>富贵鼎来即应之，鄂公未遇姑冶铁<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《栟榈先生文集》卷六）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76649'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　回故里，有诗。作品：《南归醉题家圃二首》<div id='poem_76727' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76727' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76727?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南归醉题家圃二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76727")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>六言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76727_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76727'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76727'>填海我如精卫，当车人笑螳螂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76727'>六合群黎有补，一身万段何妨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76727'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_76727_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76726' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76726' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76726?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>六言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76726_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76726'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76726'>近辅暴迫狼虎，圣君德大乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76726'>万里去黄金阙，一杯得杏花村<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《栟榈先生文集》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76726'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_76726_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　有二书《寄朱乔年》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　春，有诗。作品：《偶成三首》《贺朱乔年生日》<div id='poem_76550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76550?labeling=true' target='_blank'>偶成三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76550")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76550_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76550'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76550'>苍苔白石两清幽，缥缈虹桥跨碧流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76550'>日过窗间腾野马，雨馀墙角篆蜗牛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76550'>饥寒不作妻孥念，笑语那知天地秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76550'>一炷水沉参鼻观，扫空六凿自天游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76550'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76550_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76549?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76549'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76549'>梦破南窗袅水沉，卧看素壁挂瑶琴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76549'>丝丝细雨晚烟合，阁阁鸣蛙蔓草深。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76549'>但得瓮边眠吏部，不妨跨下辱淮阴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76549'>何时楼上登晴景，一醉聊舒万里心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76549'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76549_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76548?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76548'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76548'>万里归来卧白云，蚍蜉撼树政纷纷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76548'>大儿文举知何在，巨擘于陵亦谩云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76548'>空洞能容数百辈，蒙胧如见二三分。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76548'>小槽谁有真珠滴，径觅吾徒作半醺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76548'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76548_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺朱乔年生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76671")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76671_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76671'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76671'>三春一半入群芳，朱朱白白竞天香。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76671'>人间无处著此景，付与长庚作肺肠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76671'>长庚乘风下天宇，明窗万卷饱今古。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76671'>笔端著处皆春容，文墨林中三角虎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76671'>祇今声价高云烟，要辙故应岁九迁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76671'>便当折槛追家世，与国同休亿万年。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76671'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76671_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='23fe2487c6534a0985de7b9c464f12ae_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("23fe2487c6534a0985de7b9c464f12ae");'><span id='23fe2487c6534a0985de7b9c464f12ae_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>，33岁</div><div id='23fe2487c6534a0985de7b9c464f12ae' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　再度赴京应试，朱松有诗送别。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2df513a33917494e8953eafd3e761227_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2df513a33917494e8953eafd3e761227");'><span id='2df513a33917494e8953eafd3e761227_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1126')">1124-1126年</a>，34-36岁</div><div id='2df513a33917494e8953eafd3e761227' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　落第还乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年7月15日</a>　七月十五日，作《丹霞赏音文集序》<div id='poem_1236861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丹霞赏音文集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和七年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236861")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236861'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236861'>邵武军泰宁僧明赜走人四百里，以书抵予曰：「吾师得士大夫诗文，亡虑三百篇，雄文杰句，日传千纸，师不得以私之也，仆将镂于板，命之曰《丹霞赏音集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236861_comment'></div>夫子厚于吾师者，请为我序之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236861_comment'></div>余告之曰：若师农家子，忽有所遇，遂传心印，坐断白云，法可参，又能出其糟粕，作诗诵三昧，如画沙印泥，不事雕镌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236861_comment'></div>虽贯休、齐己等辈旬锻月鍊，有不得其彷佛者，又何待士夫为之赏音乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236861_comment'></div>而况三百篇之中，有为社稷臣者，有为文章伯者，有为道山之秀者，有为柏台之英者，有宣埋轮之威者，有布恺悌之政者，有布衣韦带而尚友古人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236861_comment'></div>钩章棘句，光芒相薄，皆不在人下，而又何待潦倒不堪者从而序之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236861_comment'></div>虽然，世间游戏法门，类相假合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236861_comment'></div>若以序为不必为，则诸公之文虽不必作可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236861_comment'></div>若以诸公之文为不必作，则丹霞之迹虽不显可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236861_comment'></div>是将颓堕委靡，荡然不可收拾，而与兔角龟毛，同归于无用之域矣，岂中道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236861_comment'></div>盖闻七佛之出世，达摩之西来，与三藏四万八千卷之流布于六合内外者，譬犹烟云出岫，本无定体，而风行水上，偶尔成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236861_comment'></div>故其建立之迹，阐扬之音，虽轰若雷声，而亦未尝不渊默也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236861_comment'></div>然则丹霞示现之迹，士夫从而赏之，明赜从而刊之，仆又从而序之，是亦循斯须矣，又孰有不可者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236861_comment'></div>丹霞法名宗本，弃妻而庵居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236861_comment'></div>得度五年，风号露泣之地化为金碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236861_comment'></div>太守请于朝以名其院，所谓「丹霞」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236861_comment'></div>世间人或得其诵者，即以吉凶寿夭决之，犹蓍龟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236861_comment'></div>此特其善者机耳，丹霞岂作意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236861_comment'></div>明赜作字吟诗，亦超然不凡，而见解的的不落一边，盖其师之嫡嗣云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236861_comment'></div>宣和七年中元，瑞芝轩书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1236861_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年11月</a>　冬，作《何长善墓志铭》<div id='poem_1236904' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236904' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236904?labeling=true' target='_blank'>何长善承事墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236904")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236904'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236904'>君讳抗，字彦高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236904_comment'></div>晋永嘉中有八姓入闽者，何其一也，君实其裔，故世为邵武桃溪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236904_comment'></div>曾父讳福，大父讳景，皇考讳绍谟，皆隐德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236904_comment'></div>自大父以下，皆博通经史，尤深《左氏春秋》，然止用以行己耳，未尝为进取计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236904_comment'></div>君继其业，家益贫，遂习进士举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236904_comment'></div>自元丰历绍圣，经义词赋，盖尝再变，君各臻其妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236904_comment'></div>抠衣膝行，愿为门弟子者，盖不特为闽中士人耳，自江以西，往往皆来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236904_comment'></div>凡辱君奖提者，类登危科，作膴仕，曳青紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236904_comment'></div>拜绛帷以谢恩德者，岁不乏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236904_comment'></div>故君虽栖迟蹭蹬，未有所遇，然声誉益砰轰，众皆意君旦夕为云霄人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236904_comment'></div>会崇宁间行舍法，月考岁计，铢积寸累，必历数寒暑，然后得以射策王庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236904_comment'></div>君曰：「嘻，吾二亲垂白，家无担石，岂可辍吾温凊不可阙之恩，以易区区无用之虚名乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236904_comment'></div>故安居陋巷，以教四方学者，鹑衣蔬茹，泰然自处，力事二亲，孝行霭闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236904_comment'></div>晚年尤喜佛书，于生死之变，盖了了然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236904_comment'></div>宣和七年冬得疾，踰月未尝伏枕，但挥肉食耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236904_comment'></div>十一月三日晨兴，正冠西首，奄然而逝，得岁六十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236904_comment'></div>娶冯氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236904_comment'></div>男二人，曰元、曰方，皆应进士举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236904_comment'></div>方尝游边，得承信郎，今陷燕，以不能归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236904_comment'></div>孙三人，曰镡、曰铸、曰铎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236904_comment'></div>元才学卓然，于某为友旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236904_comment'></div>以君门下士通直郎谢寻状君之行，不远数百里过余曰：「先君子老死场屋，不有碣铭，将泯没矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236904_comment'></div>愿夫子志之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236904_comment'></div>余曰：嘻，君终身不遇，岂才之罪乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236904_comment'></div>君少年未闻道，尝侍母疾，至于刲股。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236904_comment'></div>此在君为不足书，然孝诚所迫，非以声音笑貌为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236904_comment'></div>尝同仲兄游学江西，兄不幸，即负其骨以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236904_comment'></div>时方炎蒸，瘴疟日甚，死于道路者往往相枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236904_comment'></div>或戒君以徐行，君曰：「吁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236904_comment'></div>死生不足顾也，吾知负吾兄以慰倚门之望耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236904_comment'></div>考其所履如此，其可谓之孝子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236904_comment'></div>古人求忠臣必于孝子之门，若使君得志在朝廷上，决不顾妻孥服食之私，卖国以自媒，其所立当有绝人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236904_comment'></div>君今不忍舍其亲以居学校，遂使天下失此忠臣，盖崇宁创法者沮之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236904_comment'></div>此余所以伤一时政事之失，而不伤君之不偶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236904_comment'></div>请铭之，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1236904'>胸中万卷，笔下云烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236904_comment'></div>百不一死，归此九泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236904_comment'></div>子孙绳绳，既艺且贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236904_comment'></div>其后必大，吾卜之天。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1236904_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　春，有《沙县灵卫邓公祝文》等诗文。作品：《沙县灵卫邓公祝文》《灵卫庙赛祝愿文》《兴化重建院记》《沙县福圣院重建塔》《一枝庵记》《东林一枝庵》<div id='poem_1236908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236908?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沙县灵卫邓公祝文</a><span class='authorDate'>（靖康元年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236908")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236908_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236908'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236908'>维公昔因唐季，尝挫贼锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236908_comment'></div>脱万姓于虎牙，措一同于化国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236908_comment'></div>顷兴浙寇，共怀巢幕之危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236908_comment'></div>阴赉我邦，独享覆盂之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236908_comment'></div>使华协奏，天宠载临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236908_comment'></div>尸祝之来纷如蚁聚，庙祠之建粲若翚飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236908_comment'></div>更须左右其民，以克终始之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236908_comment'></div>英风冠世，洗空天上之旄头；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236908_comment'></div>义气横空，拥出云端之北极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236908_comment'></div>四夷电灭，六合春回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236908_comment'></div>岂惟一邑之雄，要作万邦之极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236908_comment'></div>仰希聪听，俯察舆情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236908_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1236908'>宣和八年春一月庚寅，闻金人不恭，敢拒大邦，羽檄星驰，郡邑惊扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236908_comment'></div>窃得兵符而读之，往往泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236908_comment'></div>靖康改元癸卯，夜梦有老人东向而坐，呼所统之兵，纷来无穷，皆屏息受命，无敢谁何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236908_comment'></div>老人语之曰：「若等善护此，勿挠之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236908_comment'></div>群卒皆曰：「某属于公，敢他为哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236908_comment'></div>觉而异之，曰：「是何神乎，而独祐我也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236908_comment'></div>忽郑中踵门而请曰：「灵卫被旨创庙，冠绝吾邦，出师者争祷焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236908_comment'></div>但未有祝文，幸夫子制之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236908_comment'></div>然后知灵卫公果祐吾邑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236908_comment'></div>丙午，谨撰此，录未果，而捷音到矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236908_comment'></div>天兵所指，摧朽拉枯，因其请降，舍之使去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236908_comment'></div>呜呼，快哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236908_comment'></div>叩角击壤，将复为太平民矣，遂并书之，以彰灵卫之迹云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1236908_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236909' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236909?labeling=true' target='_blank'>灵卫庙赛愿祝文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236909")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236909_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236909'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236909'>楛矢南飞，漫天如雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236909_comment'></div>左蔽江南，右暗吴越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236909_comment'></div>嗟嗟七闽，江浙之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236909_comment'></div>凛如累卵，上压太山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236909_comment'></div>我邑在闽，浪名富庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236909_comment'></div>兵火鼎来，佥曰可虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236909_comment'></div>爰率儒士，列拜庙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236909_comment'></div>冀公之庇，以窃康宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236909_comment'></div>天书夜报，贼兵稍北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236909_comment'></div>奠枕旧居，实公之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236909_comment'></div>公德如山，我不敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236909_comment'></div>既陈牲币，又奠椒浆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236909_comment'></div>君恩如天，公其可忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236909_comment'></div>既福此邦，当佐上国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236909_comment'></div>黄屋蒙尘，今犹海乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236909_comment'></div>公其相之，万国来王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236909_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1236909_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236894' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236894' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236894?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兴化重建院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236894")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236894_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236894'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236894'>余尝谓人之才术智识常生于不得已，而死于因循者，则亦偷安而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236894_comment'></div>此天下之通患，而祝发坏衣者尤甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236894_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236894_comment'></div>风雨寒暑不可以切身，鹿豕不可以杂处，饮食不具，居处不可以得众，倘未尝有寺而欲阐扬祖道者，其于创立，岂可以已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236894_comment'></div>若夫既有寺宇粗可以居，而岁月相仍，摧风烁日，主之者虽恻然作念欲一新之，徬徨四顾，曰：陋者可补也，颓者可支也，污漫者可饰也，因陋就简，吾亦可以安也，又何必尽毁旧庐，化出莲宫，然后为快于心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236894_comment'></div>因循偷安，是亦人之常情耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236894_comment'></div>南剑沙县有寺曰兴化，屹立山间，虽云简古，然建于中和之初，梵宫所当有者无或不备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236894_comment'></div>光化间，尝敕翰林以题其额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236894_comment'></div>政和末，又易律为禅，以其在闽中亦卓然号为古道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236894_comment'></div>三百年间，未闻有恶其弊者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236894_comment'></div>政和丙申，法湛主此，亦可以已矣，师乃愀然不能以自安，曰：「屋老如许，门宇萧然，亦何以为佛地哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236894_comment'></div>扶倾立仆，苟新耳目，琐琐然一二治之，非吾志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236894_comment'></div>于是即寺之左，得地爽垲，斩茅焚翳，乃迁故址。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236894_comment'></div>顾虽斋庖索然，殆不能烟，亦未尝过计，缩身节口益坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236894_comment'></div>今力得匠者数十人，乃躬自执爨，如事其师，虽风雨迷天，弗顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236894_comment'></div>诚心旁达，乡井翕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236894_comment'></div>由是富者出财，壮者竭力，百日之间，辇土运材，有至于三千指者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236894_comment'></div>故阅十年而寺成，巍然中立，危栋翚飞，欲凌霄汉，堂堂塑像，亦妙绝一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236894_comment'></div>为堂于上者二，内而晏寝，外而演法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236894_comment'></div>为堂于下者三，以供罗汉，以斋水陆，以饭缁素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236894_comment'></div>香积有厨，声钟有楼，翼之以廊，而重之以门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236894_comment'></div>左右前后，绳绳翼翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236894_comment'></div>计寺内外既无毫发不具，其雄丽庄严又非前寺所能彷佛，而尺椽片瓦俱出师力，未尝取用旧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236894_comment'></div>呜呼，难矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236894_comment'></div>是可以因循而不因循者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236894_comment'></div>其勉勉自克，志力俱到，当于前辈求之，故余因其求记，乃详为书焉，且以为怠惰委靡者之戒云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236894_comment'></div>师初建法堂，石其基者再，凡再圮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236894_comment'></div>师忧甚，忽省往时梦建是寺，有庞眉皓发者告之曰：「寺基更深二尺许，乃真道场」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236894_comment'></div>尝试辟之，恍如梦中，又得石柱六以建殿宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236894_comment'></div>有足痕者尺馀，在石柱之阴，见者皆云「此佛迹也，非雕镌所能至」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236894_comment'></div>此寺之兴，所以神速如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236894_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236894_comment'></div>梦中之境，变灭须臾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236894_comment'></div>石中之迹，千古不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236894_comment'></div>其将以梦为虚，而以石为实乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236894_comment'></div>通乎昼夜，本无二理，石固非实，而梦亦非虚也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236894_comment'></div>梦中占梦，师固未暇，然既赖此以兴寺，要了此以为寺之所以兴，故余并为师论之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1236894_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236893' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236893' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236893?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沙县福圣院重建塔记</a><span class='authorDate'>（靖康元年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236893")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236893_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236893'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236893'>塔寺之建，自罽宾国始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236893_comment'></div>举国之大，不过二所，佛氏且从而赞之，以为希有事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236893_comment'></div>然则佛塔岂可多得耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236893_comment'></div>唐武后欲创祠于白马坡，张廷圭力谏曰：「穷山之木以为塔，不足高也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236893_comment'></div>后乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236893_comment'></div>然则佛塔岂易建耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236893_comment'></div>然近年以来，井邑盛处必有浮屠，计天下之大，当以万数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236893_comment'></div>难易多寡，何相绝如此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236893_comment'></div>岂今日佛教之盛，非昔者比乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236893_comment'></div>抑天下富庶，而土木之功易于创造乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236893_comment'></div>余尝疑其说，以质诸长老，曰：「凡建造者，为殿以供佛，为堂以供僧，为桥为路以通往来，是各有所为，而非偶然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236893_comment'></div>独浮屠之建，动切星汉，其功甚劳，其费不赀，而于僧徒未见其有益焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236893_comment'></div>然则古今所以难之而不欲多建者，岂非为是耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236893_comment'></div>长老曰：「不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236893_comment'></div>此庄严之道也，今人未必非而古人未必是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236893_comment'></div>今夫假木石之功，而饰以丹青之丽，光芒璀璨，卓然出井邑之上，凡有目者皆见而仰之曰：佛菩萨舍其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236893_comment'></div>凡十人睹之，而一人能作正念，则千而百、万而千，展转不穷，当有不可以数计者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236893_comment'></div>是则庄严之胜以五采说法，而观瞻之士得以目听之，其助教化固不小矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236893_comment'></div>而谓之无益，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236893_comment'></div>此阿育王之建塔所以至八万四千，而佛氏而不以为多也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236893_comment'></div>南剑之沙县有寺曰福圣，古道场也，三朝宸翰，实镇其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236893_comment'></div>古塔中立，盖累数百年，舞风沐雨，望之黔闇，不足以耸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236893_comment'></div>住持僧端一毅然撤去，曰：「吾将协众力以新之」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236893_comment'></div>铢积寸累，殆十馀岁，斲削之功仅十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236893_comment'></div>三易主僧，事益因循，塔忽倒影在密室中，虽雨旸弗变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236893_comment'></div>众复骇之，益加重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236893_comment'></div>大丞相李公为之浓墨大字以题其额，又录宣和褒封之制，而继之以泗滨惊世之迹，刊于塔右，将以诲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236893_comment'></div>适公还朝，而主僧之志老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236893_comment'></div>建安郭侯来宰是邑，乃喟然而叹曰：「君父遗迹既臣子所不敢易，而塔庙之设乃遗迹之所托者也，于此不竭力焉，恐非人臣之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236893_comment'></div>谚曰：作浮屠者必合其尖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236893_comment'></div>将以合之，舍我而谁哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236893_comment'></div>于是率邑人之彦者告以故，且令主僧了机从而奔走之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236893_comment'></div>故富者出财，能者竭力，亹亹相劝，殆有不能以自已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236893_comment'></div>阅明年而塔成，实靖康改元之春也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236893_comment'></div>其级五，其广四十有八尺，而高三十丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236893_comment'></div>云烟缥缈之间，金碧相照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236893_comment'></div>夜灯数枝，焕如星斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236893_comment'></div>呜呼盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236893_comment'></div>岂特使百里之内迁善于观瞻之际，而悔过于杳冥之间乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236893_comment'></div>三后之志且不废于海滨，而云汉之章人天共仰，盖将与日俱新矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236893_comment'></div>夫仰而事君，俯而化民，今一举而两得之，其可谓贤令尹哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236893_comment'></div>余适罪逐还乡，与观胜事，侯乃以记文见属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236893_comment'></div>余曰：嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236893_comment'></div>昔韩愈氏必欲火佛氏之书而庐其居，然后为快于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236893_comment'></div>至僧澄观能造浮屠于淮泗之上，栏柱雄丽，高三百尺，愈遂作诗以美之，且谓当时公才吏用无如师者，遂令澄观之名同愈不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236893_comment'></div>得非宝塔之建，于有为佛事为甚难，顾虽倔强如韩子者，亦不得以却之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236893_comment'></div>今庄严是塔而主其寺者，僧惠深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236893_comment'></div>具正大法眼，为达摩嫡嗣，非若澄观所能髣髴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236893_comment'></div>余尝从之论西来意，又非若退之以谈佛为讳者，固愿以笔墨赞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236893_comment'></div>而况邑大夫切切外护之志在君与民，又于予为诗酒之旧，见而属之勤至于再三者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236893_comment'></div>此皆余所乐书者，敢以不才辞？</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1236893_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236898?labeling=true' target='_blank'>一枝庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236898")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236898_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236898'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236898'>余少年喜水，凿井穴地，泛溪钓月，终日潺湲之乐，盖将安焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236898_comment'></div>曰：「水止是矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236898_comment'></div>或者曰：「是未尝见江、河、淮、济也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236898_comment'></div>比年奔走道路，偶皆见之，汪洋万顷，茫无涯涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236898_comment'></div>若风作其上，则澎湃汗漫，浪高银屋，然后知余前日之喜，止牛蹄泓者耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236898_comment'></div>或者又曰：「此亦未足以言水也，是特四渎之分耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236898_comment'></div>若大海，则会而纳之六合，内外通为一流，岂啻万川而已哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236898_comment'></div>余曰：「嘻，有是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236898_comment'></div>余将游焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236898_comment'></div>客曰：「是乌能遍耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236898_comment'></div>天地之大，各五亿五万五千五百里，而四海为之脉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236898_comment'></div>今欲登穷发，游聂耳，以极无穷之观，非肉飞八极不可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236898_comment'></div>余乃茫然自失，仰而叹曰：「天下之景无穷，而玩景之情亦无尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236898_comment'></div>任情逐景，不知归宿，其将为波流乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236898_comment'></div>尝观涓涓之微，升于天，行于地，运乎千古，曾无损益，于此了之，则当体而足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236898_comment'></div>满空之水，固无异于一滴耳，亦何必沧海乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236898_comment'></div>脱或不然，而必欲赏之，又有大于此者，则将如之何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236898_comment'></div>呜呼，岂特观水为然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236898_comment'></div>天下之事，类皆如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236898_comment'></div>夏屋广殿，金碧相照，鸣钟伐鼓，食指数万，此释氏之居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236898_comment'></div>领其寺者，指顾之间，方袍云集，作止寝食，无不可意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236898_comment'></div>其视安居老人，蒙头冷坐，饮水采薇，无曰相万乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236898_comment'></div>虽然，不能安居而必欲领寺，若以寺为未足，则如之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236898_comment'></div>世间轻煖肥甘，迷楼琼屋，不知几万等，吾又安能足其志耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236898_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236898_comment'></div>芬芬鼎烹，要在满腹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236898_comment'></div>沈沈府居，要在驻足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236898_comment'></div>一庵之大，固有馀地矣，又何事他求哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236898_comment'></div>庄周曰：「鹪鹩巢于深林，不过一枝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236898_comment'></div>善乎，庄周之能了此意也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236898_comment'></div>且不了一滴之旨，虽倾四海之流不足以供其赏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236898_comment'></div>不悟一枝之要，虽扩六合之大不足以厌其求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236898_comment'></div>此世士所以终身汩汩，荡荡忘返，可以深嗟而叹息也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236898_comment'></div>妙智大师美公，少年学医，法造三昧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236898_comment'></div>稍壮则事潜庵，求西来意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236898_comment'></div>精进敏惠，便为一时名僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236898_comment'></div>若肯降志以悦当路，则巨刹名寺，当尽付之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236898_comment'></div>师乃恬然曾不介意，是故求医之人布施山积，师尽捐之，以作佛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236898_comment'></div>尝托迹太平寺，适遭回禄，尺椽不具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236898_comment'></div>二十年间，栋宇轮奂，冠于一邑，师之力盖居其半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236898_comment'></div>事母最孝，无愧古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236898_comment'></div>忽失所恃，则欲谢医术，曰：「吾不复事此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236898_comment'></div>既毕襄奉，则作庵墓侧，为终焉计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236898_comment'></div>其视同参子丽服雄居，沛然得意，但知如涕唾耳，岂非了此一滴，遂能安此一枝乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236898_comment'></div>故余字其庵曰一枝庵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236898_comment'></div>客有问曰：「居庵之士当以亿计，岂皆了此乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1236898_comment'></div>余曰：「不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1236898_comment'></div>世人有才学智术不足以动人者，退居茅舍，盖其分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1236898_comment'></div>幸而有学问，语言粗可应对，又平居交游无显人膴仕，虽欲舍庵，又将焉适？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1236898_comment'></div>此特系焉而止耳，岂皆悟此理耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1236898_comment'></div>其性识超然出人伦等，士夫喜师不可胜计，于此安之，不有觊觎，是真了此者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1236898_comment'></div>虽然，列子行天，非风不可，古人讥之，盖非无待而然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1236898_comment'></div>今师必赖一枝，犹未脱焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1236898_comment'></div>百尺竿头，当进一步，师肯承当否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1236898_comment'></div>更俟他日与师分付。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1236898_comment'></div>师名仁美，南剑州沙县人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1236898_comment'></div>庵在县之南，起于宣和之季，落成于靖康之初云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1236898_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76576' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76576?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东林一枝庵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76576")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76576_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76576'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76576'>世间杰栋俯飞翰，帘旌不动天风寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76576'>但得一身自安逸，谁思寒士三万间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76576'>东林天下推第一，净几明窗万禅客。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76576'>主人幽栖仅一枝，便觉宽容无迫窄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76576'>一身六尺何足患，蠢动当知俱欲安。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76576'>谁识曹溪一滴许，能令法雨遍尘寰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76576'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76576_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　清明节，有《栖云日新轩记》<div id='poem_1236895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236895?labeling=true' target='_blank'>栖云日新轩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（靖康元年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236895")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236895_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236895'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236895'>自西晋以下，祝发坏衣之禁弛于中国，故四海内外，江山胜处，皆释子居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236895_comment'></div>凡居寺以领众者，孰不欲峻治其宇，以阐扬此道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236895_comment'></div>凡临事之初，必踌躇四顾，曰：吾所有者如何，求于人者如何，事成若否，其利害劳逸又如何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236895_comment'></div>故其决然欲为之志，已夺于衰惫不果之气矣，事岂复有济耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236895_comment'></div>幸而有气宇不凡、断然若将有为者，又其经营措置，颠倒错乱，或急其所宜缓，而后其所当先，顾虽疲精竭力，亦徒自纷纷耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236895_comment'></div>此败椽老屋所以颓圮日甚，可以深嗟而屡叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236895_comment'></div>故余尝论天下事曰：有欲为之志者，未必有敢为之气；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236895_comment'></div>有敢为之气者，未必有能为之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236895_comment'></div>三者备矣，虽天下可宰也，况一寺之小乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236895_comment'></div>或阙一焉，虽八口之家亦有不充者，况一寺之众乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236895_comment'></div>沙县栖云，古禅刹也，堂宇卑陋，仅庇风雨，盖不知几百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236895_comment'></div>真戒大师可臣以百丈法居之，才三年，余往造焉，见其翚飞栋宇，屹立寺东，所谓库院者新矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236895_comment'></div>明年过之，则见其金碧相照，恍若莲宫，所谓如来宝殿者新矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236895_comment'></div>越三年又过之，见其函轴星布，机缄雷动，庄严之胜，如天造地设，所谓宝藏新矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236895_comment'></div>余固信若人之奇者也，且度其力必穷矣，非息肩数十年，恐不敢议若事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236895_comment'></div>近年过之，则又见其立殿于藏之右，以奉传经者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236895_comment'></div>架堂于殿之下，以居阅经者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236895_comment'></div>辟宇于殿之上，以娱游息者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236895_comment'></div>又创云会堂于藏之左，渠渠夏屋，可居数百众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236895_comment'></div>草芥泉石之间，丹雘焕然，又一新也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236895_comment'></div>计寺内外当不复可以措手矣，而良材山积，瓦甓鳞比，又若有为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236895_comment'></div>因诘之，对曰：「法堂斋厨今虽亡恙，然数年新创已杰立云霄间，此不得以独卑也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236895_comment'></div>意必尽新之而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236895_comment'></div>余惊问其故，曰：「若岁所入几何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236895_comment'></div>曰：「聊尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236895_comment'></div>「求于人者几何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236895_comment'></div>曰：「未尝遣化士」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236895_comment'></div>「然则斤斧之声积今十年不绝，而土木之工鼎来未艾，使游赏之客每见而益新，是何自而然哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236895_comment'></div>曰：「缩身节口，铢积寸进，亦随缘耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236895_comment'></div>余盖知真戒之志之气之才，果有绝人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236895_comment'></div>乃与之坐于小轩之上，作终日款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236895_comment'></div>师以轩榜为请，予故字之曰「日新」，盖记所见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236895_comment'></div>有客难之曰：「此寺之兴十八年矣，真戒之力可以唾手而就，期以一二年间，无可新者，后日过之，无乃辜吾子命名之意乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236895_comment'></div>余曰：「嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236895_comment'></div>此特真戒之馀事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236895_comment'></div>渠得法于雪峰，见闻的的，出人数等，故步陈迹，一切扫去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236895_comment'></div>盖尝与之语，亦无时而不新也，岂止创立之功哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236895_comment'></div>客无以对，余于是并书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236895_comment'></div>靖康改元清明记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1236895_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年3月15日</a>　三月中旬，因李纲等荐，召赴阙，赐进士出身，补承务郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年3月</a>　是月，有《答张居实》书。<div id='poem_1236846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答张居实书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236846")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236846'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236846'>某顿首再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236846_comment'></div>久别，辱书，开缄如见君子，宠喻详备，非爱人以德者不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236846_comment'></div>某何人，当宣和之末，见九州需索，东南一空，而花石之奉鼎沸无已，学校诸生仰瞻白云，俱相顾泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236846_comment'></div>且自度曰：圣天子未尝杀一谏臣，士大夫吞声端坐，愿固位耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236846_comment'></div>偶得数章，槌鼓以进，虽为齑粉，不顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236846_comment'></div>圣意包荒，未赐诛殛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236846_comment'></div>今得邸报，乃有召命，是将责我以前日未死之躯，以为今日报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236846_comment'></div>白日尚在，赤心敢渝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236846_comment'></div>区区牛、李，岂所学哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236846_comment'></div>异时有违此语，公当出之，则仆有何面目更行天日之下耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236846_comment'></div>反覆来书，盖知己者，以报公所以不得不尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236846_comment'></div>春且老，传道佳胜，未见，幸为吾道自寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236846_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1236846_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年4月23日</a>　仍居乡未赴诏命。有《题称老开堂疏》<div id='poem_1236881' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236881' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236881?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题称老开堂疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（靖康元年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236881")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236881_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236881'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236881'>称老挂锡延平广教，禅悦之馀，闭户读书，时出好语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236881_comment'></div>使君太博庄公闻而喜之，令居天王，为制疏文，有「神珠法雨」之语，可谓知称者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236881_comment'></div>称今领众肃然，日传此道，清誉四播，如走风雷，亦可谓不负使君所知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236881_comment'></div>德公之赐，欲刊其疏，且求某跋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236881_comment'></div>余以谓欲报其德者，不必刊其文，然非托于文则无以志吾之知遇也，于是乎书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236881_comment'></div>靖康改元四月己未，栟榈某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1236881_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年5月</a>　朝廷十一次催促，始拟赴任。有《答陈梦兆》书。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='774bdd0ee4b1484fae7494ff51c2551e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("774bdd0ee4b1484fae7494ff51c2551e");'><span id='774bdd0ee4b1484fae7494ff51c2551e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1128')">1127-1128年</a>，37-38岁</div><div id='774bdd0ee4b1484fae7494ff51c2551e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年10月</a>　十月，罢左正言，回归乡里。其堂弟志中作《亦骥轩记》<div id='poem_1236889' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236889' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236889?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亦骥轩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236889")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236889_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236889'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236889'>余谪自左掖，远归里闬，志中出郭四十馀里迓余于高砂邮亭，再拜而起曰：「兄以言事召，复以言事出，职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236889_comment'></div>脱身虏营，驱驰万里，遂得以拜亲闱，幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236889_comment'></div>谨以贺」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236889_comment'></div>复再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236889_comment'></div>予喜其言，似有所见者，岂三二年间学问自进耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236889_comment'></div>吁，可喜也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236889_comment'></div>志中相别，闻嗜酒喜游，浮沈里巷中，似未能自克者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236889_comment'></div>至于好贤乐善之心，则不啻若饥渴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236889_comment'></div>然予固尝远期之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236889_comment'></div>今日闻见，果非故吾，是不负余所期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236889_comment'></div>推是心以往，则亦何所不至哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236889_comment'></div>志中乃归治其室，环列今古，闭户静坐，虽居陋巷而享箪瓢，泰如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236889_comment'></div>予过之，而字其轩曰亦骥轩，且语之曰：「『晞骥之马，亦骥之乘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236889_comment'></div>晞颜之人，亦颜之徒』，此扬雄氏之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236889_comment'></div>回之道非常常然者，雄以骥比之，岂称其德而不称其力欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236889_comment'></div>且夫气逸神骏，蔑视燕、越，长鸣就道，箭激电飞，此骥之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236889_comment'></div>至于俛首羁缰，以安服御，载上之勤，夷险不变，此非以其德欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236889_comment'></div>回在洙泗之间，以言语则不如宰我、子贡，以政事则不如冉有、子路，以文学则不如子游、子夏，其所以卓然冠于三子之徒而居四科之首者，盖在此而不在彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236889_comment'></div>志中有志于若人乎，即此晞之，是知本矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236889_comment'></div>虽然，晞骥可能也，而亦骥不可能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236889_comment'></div>晞骥云者，特有志焉而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236889_comment'></div>至于亦骥，则己行其所至，与之齐驱并驾，殆有不可得而优劣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236889_comment'></div>余所以命轩之名者大矣，予所以期志中者高且远矣，志中其勉之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236889_comment'></div>异日无愧于此轩之名，斯无愧于乃兄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236889_comment'></div>若无愧于乃兄，则步骖齐驱，殆未可以今日量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236889_comment'></div>会有伯乐，为子一顾，岂久困盐车者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236889_comment'></div>志中其勉之」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236889_comment'></div>志中名昼，于予为弟云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1236889_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年10月</a>　被贬回乡后有诗。作品：《偶题》《次韵二首》<div id='poem_76515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76515")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76515'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76515'>玉殿曾叨侍冕旒，才疏意广误旁求。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76515'>汇征那敢私连茹，勇退何妨在急流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76515'>蓬荜已无原宪室，江山要饱子长游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76515'>西庵轩槛多风月，幸子时来共茗瓯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76515_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76515'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76515_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76514?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76514'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76514'>怪底祥光夜满门，朝来入社得诗人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76514'>空疏嗟我句无眼，俊逸知君笔有神。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76514'>共隐兵戈不到处，相携云水自由身。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76514'>便当痛饮追河朔，红雪缤纷脍锦鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76514'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　被贬回乡后所写。作品：《答吴时中》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年2月</a>　为文祭陈瓘。作品：《奉安陈谏议祭文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《两宋词人丛考》本。）</span><div id='poem_1236906' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236906' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236906?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉安陈谏议祭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎三年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236906")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236906_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236906'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236906'>维建炎三年岁次戊申，二月乙卯朔，二十日甲戌，某谨以清酌庶羞之奠，昭告故谏议大夫了斋先生陈公之灵曰：靖康之难，胎于崇宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236906_comment'></div>相彼元恶，治乱已分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236906_comment'></div>人皆见于已著，公独察乎未形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236906_comment'></div>正色立朝，上撄逆鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236906_comment'></div>虽菽粟之奉不给于朝昏，而正直之气盖充塞乎乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236906_comment'></div>若上皇能用公于三黜之后，则必无宣和之末；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236906_comment'></div>若渊圣能作公于九泉之下，则必无沙漠之征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236906_comment'></div>呜呼，已矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236906_comment'></div>公道兴衰，系国休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236906_comment'></div>故公之死生存亡，不系乎公而系乎造物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236906_comment'></div>昔公南迁，义不枉尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236906_comment'></div>斯民企踵，犹冀万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236906_comment'></div>一旦梦奠于两楹之间，四海为之失色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236906_comment'></div>善类无归，吾道将绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236906_comment'></div>小人无畏，争臣新室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236906_comment'></div>此有志之士所以为天下恸，而不独为邦人惜也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236906_comment'></div>圣人念公，恩锡日隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236906_comment'></div>平生事业，已勒鼎钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236906_comment'></div>乡曲儒生，慕公高风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236906_comment'></div>参前倚衡，若接音容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236906_comment'></div>貌公之像，血食学宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236906_comment'></div>先圣之道，与公无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236906_comment'></div>尚享！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1236906_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年3月</a>　沙县重修儒学，为作记。作品：《沙县重修县学记》<div id='poem_1236887' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236887' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236887?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沙阳重修县学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236887")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236887_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236887'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236887'>余尝怪道、释之居，雄丽相胜，而州县之学类不足以方之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236887_comment'></div>顾其无自而然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236887_comment'></div>盖人心役役，不有所贪，则必有所惧，未尝有斯须宁者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236887_comment'></div>道家者流曰：我能荐人于天，可以几福于式外，故贪者慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236887_comment'></div>释氏者流曰：我能福人于九泉之下，虽造业深重者，鬼亦不得以诛之，故凡有罪者惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236887_comment'></div>贪者利其如此，而惧者以惟恐其不我利也，此道、释之宫所以轮奂奇胜，殆遍天下，非学宫比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236887_comment'></div>崇宁以来，蔡京为冢宰，群天下学者纳之黉舍，校其文艺，等为三品，饮食之给，因而有差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236887_comment'></div>旌别人才，止付于鱼肉铢两间，学者不以为羞，且逐逐然贪之曰：吾利在是，不可一日舍是而他也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236887_comment'></div>县有帅长，郡有教授，未必知有所谓学校之本者，但务为美观耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236887_comment'></div>帅使者又从而督之，以学宫成坏为州县殿最，斥叱所及，官吏胆落，故士夫惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236887_comment'></div>此崇宁间学舍之盛，所以妙绝今古，可以无愧于道、释之宫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236887_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236887_comment'></div>学校之兴虽自崇宁，而学校之废政由崇宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236887_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236887_comment'></div>盖设教之意专以禄养为重轻，则学校之士岂复顾义哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236887_comment'></div>知有利心而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236887_comment'></div>一旦赫然复祖宗法，以科举取士，学者则曰朝廷不以学校观我矣，吾何贪焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236887_comment'></div>州县则曰部使者不以学校督我矣，吾何惧焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236887_comment'></div>是故昔日青衿接迹弦歌之地，今则败椽老屋，号风泣露，使人过之凄凄然如墟墓间，若不可以复振者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236887_comment'></div>是真可伤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236887_comment'></div>南剑有邑曰沙县，溪山之胜，文物之盛，盖甲于一郡，其在闽中，亦号为卓卓然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236887_comment'></div>舍法既罢，学校亦废，仰雨傍风，儒生扫迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236887_comment'></div>宣和七年，建安郭侯得邑于此，恻然作念曰：此邦亦复如是耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236887_comment'></div>舍法可罢，学校不可罢，置而弗顾，非为政之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236887_comment'></div>于是邦人之彦者，率侯之语，各竭力以营之，朝夕勉勉，若切其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236887_comment'></div>曾未踰时，讲者有堂，居者有舍，奉先圣者有殿，斋宫祭具，无不备器，栋宇凌空，朱碧相照，又有非崇宁间所能及者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236887_comment'></div>于是学者偕来，啾啾訚訚，有洙泗之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236887_comment'></div>呜呼盛哉，古无有也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236887_comment'></div>殆不知大夫与邦人之彦者惧使者之督而肯为之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236887_comment'></div>抑贪夫所谓三舍之选而为之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236887_comment'></div>内无所贪，外无所惧，上下相率，必于有成，果何谓哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236887_comment'></div>一言以蔽之曰：诚心而已矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236887_comment'></div>然则郭侯之志与邦人之彦者，岂不既贤矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1236887_comment'></div>余于建炎之初论事谪自左掖，因以冷居里闬，盖将束书负琴，日造庠序，以为废事之愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1236887_comment'></div>侯乃以记文见属，余曰：「唯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1236887_comment'></div>此仆所愿附姓名者，敢不书」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1236887_comment'></div>虽然，学宫之弊今已新之，寒暑相易，风雨摧剥，异时能保其不弊耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1236887_comment'></div>侯文章事业，霭闻于时，牛刀割鸡，岂久留此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1236887_comment'></div>弊而复新，其在邦人之诚心乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1236887_comment'></div>且诚之为道大矣，天地可动也，金石可革也，惟出于至诚，则有确乎其不可易者，顾其勤于今日，而怠于后日者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1236887_comment'></div>异时郭公持节以过旧部，若见学宫不减今日，然后知至诚之道可亘千古，非贪与惧者之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1236887_comment'></div>故余并书之，以告来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1236887_comment'></div>侯字舜卿，汝贤其名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1236887_comment'></div>学兴于庆历二年春二月有二日，而新于宣和七年冬十月二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1236887_comment'></div>建炎二年三月吉时立<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1236887_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1236887'>「侯字」至「吉时立」数句，原无，据同治《沙县志》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1236887_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1236887'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_44_1236887_0'>⑴ 《栟榈集》卷一六。又见《永乐大典》卷二一九八三，同治《沙县志》卷六。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1236887_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年3月</a>　沙县新建三清殿，为作记。作品：《新建三清殿记》<div id='poem_1236891' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>新建三清殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236891")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236891_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236891'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236891'>闽水曲折，行乱石间，鼎烹雪喷，相应而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236891_comment'></div>独沙邑有溪广千馀尺，纡馀舒缓，湛如青铜，其远至于二十馀里，不闻湍激声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236891_comment'></div>南有七峰，草木苍然，四时不改；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236891_comment'></div>北列万井，楼阁翚飞，不可以数计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236891_comment'></div>昔令尹自县治而南，方舟为梁，径抵七峰之最西者，辟山为堂，瞰危为阁，下俯风雨，旁列星辰，似非尘寰中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236891_comment'></div>盖沙邑据闽中之胜，而是堂与阁又据沙邑之胜，此登赏之士所以冠盖相望，而游宦于此者尤切切焉，若以不得款于是者为大可恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236891_comment'></div>今令尹郭侯见而叹曰：「嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236891_comment'></div>此胜景也，是真可喜者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236891_comment'></div>虽然，有家焉必有仰事俯育之计，有职焉必有民社之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236891_comment'></div>今为家者弃其家以嬉，为职者舍其职以嬉，举邑之人若狂焉，无乃以胜景为累乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236891_comment'></div>于是呼道士张唐的居之，凿山作殿，中设三清像，巍巍堂堂，与阁相称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236891_comment'></div>昔日妖歌曼舞之地，今化为歛笏垂绅之宫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236891_comment'></div>昔日穷奢极欲之境，今化为悔罪忏非之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236891_comment'></div>昔者邑官晏此以虐天子之民，今也邑官叩此以请天子之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236891_comment'></div>是非善恶，岂不相万乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236891_comment'></div>郭侯此举，其可谓卓然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236891_comment'></div>且叩予门，请以文记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236891_comment'></div>予筮仕之初，尝待罪鸿胪寺，道、释二教，兼所辖者，其记之为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236891_comment'></div>且尝因贱职之简，得以考其教之所自来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236891_comment'></div>其源出黄帝，其道再盛于老聃，其末流诡异，有真可骇者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236891_comment'></div>其为家三十有七，其为书九百九十有三篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236891_comment'></div>凡有天下者，必崇其道，论其尤者有三帝焉：秦曰始皇，汉曰武帝，唐曰明皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236891_comment'></div>是三帝者才智绝人，蔑视一世，穷六合之大不足以厌其欲，于是浩然有御风骑气之志，炼丹飞符，杂以左道，自谓其法可配天地，殊不知飞腾之术卒不能济，反祸其国，真可痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236891_comment'></div>此学孔子者所以不欲言老聃氏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236891_comment'></div>虽然，汉高祖之取天下，则以张良为最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236891_comment'></div>其治天下也，则以曹参为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236891_comment'></div>良之道盖慕赤松子，而参之居则避正室以舍盖公，是则道家之术，又若无负于天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236891_comment'></div>盖汉高祖所以取参与良者，在道之本不过于清净恭俭无为，与民息肩而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236891_comment'></div>而始皇、武帝、明皇之所尚者，区区竭力以事其末，故诞妄不经者得以行其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236891_comment'></div>其治乱贤否所以相绝，不可同日而语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236891_comment'></div>今郭侯崇奉之志既在其本，此吾所以记之不敢辄辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236891_comment'></div>夫末流滋蔓，变怪百出，可以惑人主而祸天下者，皆非黄帝、老聃氏之道也，予固尝斥之矣，奚独孟子能辟杨、朱哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1236891_comment'></div>当有辨之者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1236891_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　春，有诗与知县郭汝贤唱和。作品：《与郭舜钦朝请》《次韵郭宰兼简丞尉三首》<div class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76565")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76565'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76565'>成均冷坐穷吞纸，额叩龙墀滨九死。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76565'>背负琴书偶生还，赖有春风满故里。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76565'>故里渺居天一隅，因仍蔓草不堪除。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76565'>多谢先生肯游刃，号令雷霆一扫驱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76565'>旧弊忽消新庆长，老稚相携纷击壤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76565'>坐使牛蹄一泓中，九万共抟羊角上。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76565'>只恐朝廷急英雄，割鸡不用烦屠龙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76565'>政须太山来压卵，金阙唤回小令公。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76565'>陋巷嗟余空四壁，饿死平生无枉尺。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76565'>知音今有昌黎公，玉川得卧三竿日。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76565'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_76565_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76524?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵郭宰兼简丞尉三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_76524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76524'>六合便当归化笔，一同聊复赏澄江。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76523'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76523'>只将诗律对晴窗，我本无为人自降。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76523_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76523'>曹子棒头施色五，崔侯厅下植松双。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76523_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76523'>千篇堪友骑鲸李，八咏当奴梦笔江。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76523_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76523'>文字兴馀行乐耳，肯容碧玉自盈缸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76523_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76523'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76523_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_76522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76522'>见闻仅得豹斑一，胜负犹争蛙角双。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76522_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76522'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76522_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　春，有诗。作品：《洪丞和来再次韵》《成彦女奴琵琶》《寄璨老西轩》<div id='poem_76539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76539'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76539'>堂堂国士洪夫子，刻烛从渠心自降。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' target='_blank'>寄璨老西轩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃",
