id='poem_sentence_1_76553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76553'>祇今得兔不钻纸，那用浮杯更度江。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76553'>前世远公只师是，好从元亮供千缸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76553'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76553_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='20fb7a8a5108446bb659d9cac31e1e74_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("20fb7a8a5108446bb659d9cac31e1e74");'><span id='20fb7a8a5108446bb659d9cac31e1e74_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1130')">1128-1130年</a>，38-40岁</div><div id='20fb7a8a5108446bb659d9cac31e1e74' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　年底，回沙县。有诗。作品：《过黄杨岩》<div id='poem_76696' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76696' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76696?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄杨岩<span class='inlineComment2'>（万历本题作同冯阳游黄杨岩）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76696")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76696'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76696'>石壁巉岩惊鬼划，异草幽花锁春色。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76696'>群山迤逦不能高，突兀独磨霄汉碧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76696'>芒鞋千尺上崔嵬，手摘星辰脚底雷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76696'>拨破烟云得洞户，醉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>眼恐是天门开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76696'>入门嵯峨森紫玉，冷风吹面天香馥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76696'>箕踞胡床<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>挥麈尾，万指未充空洞腹。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76696'>我因避地访名山，扁舟夜渡沙溪寒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76696'>辛勤博此一笑喜，太平犹在水云间。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76696'>猛将今无三角虎，狐狸昼号鳅鳝舞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76696'>灵岩知有老龙藏，挽出人间作霖雨。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76696'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_76696'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_76696_0'>⑴ 原字缺坏，据道光本、曹抄补</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_76696_0'>⑵ 箕、床二字原缺，据道光本、曹抄补</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_76696_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月21日</a>　吕之望建堂纪念李纲，为作记。作品：《具瞻堂记》<div id='poem_1236888' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236888' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236888?labeling=true' target='_blank'>具瞻堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎三年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236888")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236888_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236888'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236888'>大丞相李公宣和初以左史论时事之失，谪监沙邑筦库，期年而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236888_comment'></div>宣和末，以奉常还朝，与决大计，遂参左辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236888_comment'></div>虏骑迫城，公以身蔽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236888_comment'></div>虏退，迁元枢，未几而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236888_comment'></div>虏骑再至，则汴都不守矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236888_comment'></div>今上即位之初，走使召公，再迁为左仆射，纪律稍正，群盗向息，而公又逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236888_comment'></div>不数月间，翠华有维扬之幸，故天下识与不识，皆谓公之出入，系朝廷重轻，非近世名臣所可比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236888_comment'></div>东坡曰：「儿童诵君实，走卒知司马」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236888_comment'></div>吾今于公复见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236888_comment'></div>新安吕子之望，以智谋中科，得官九品，筮仕之初，袭公筦库之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236888_comment'></div>一日，居其堂而四顾曰：「此非大丞相李公之所憩乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236888_comment'></div>平日仰公如太山北斗，今以职事继公后尘，其瞻仰之诚，参前倚衡，如见公于上，虽食息謦欬之顷，不敢辄忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236888_comment'></div>请新其堂，而榜之曰具瞻，所以致仆拳拳之诚，且与后来有知者共之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236888_comment'></div>堂成，予即造焉，虽喜吕子趋向不凡，且为吕子危之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236888_comment'></div>李公直气充塞天壤，不能一日安其身于朝廷之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236888_comment'></div>当时愿留之者殆以万计，几坑于奸佞之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236888_comment'></div>有抗章以挽之者，皆斥窜流离、去朝廷数千里者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236888_comment'></div>至于枭首通衢，以竦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236888_comment'></div>吕子何恃，而敢如此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236888_comment'></div>予窃为吕子危之，因以告之曰：「前日死谏之士，今此去国之臣，皆子从游之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236888_comment'></div>当时议论，子无不与者，朝廷大臣盖已切齿，但未有以发之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236888_comment'></div>故去年省试，子虽优擢，有司观望，吹毛求疵，竟不复廷对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236888_comment'></div>今不省愆易虑，默默安职，复尔作为，是自贻咎耳，后悔其将追乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236888_comment'></div>吕子曰：「诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236888_comment'></div>坐此获罪，芬芳多矣，谨俟之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236888_comment'></div>建炎三年二月二十一日记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236888_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1236888'>某不善作真字，记成而不能书，畏祸患者又不肯书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236888_comment'></div>建安张博见而喜曰：「李公之德卓卓如许，岂独吕子愿游其门哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236888_comment'></div>仆请书之，祸福之来，吾弗计也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236888_comment'></div>噫，世间惟不计祸福者，方可与论出处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236888_comment'></div>某今又何幸而得与二子同游乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1236888_comment'></div>后五日，某题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1236888_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年7月7日</a>　七月，作《瑞花堂序》<div id='poem_1236860' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236860' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236860?labeling=true' target='_blank'>瑞花堂序</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎三年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236860")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236860_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236860'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236860'>政和间，有瑞花生于叶隆吉超然家，状如牡丹，红莹不谢，而未尝有根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236860_comment'></div>众虽异之，竟不知其为何物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236860_comment'></div>超然一旦抱其所能，贡入成均，且十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236860_comment'></div>靖康间，以智谋中科得官，未试；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236860_comment'></div>建炎二年，再擢进士第，易紫衣蓝，归拜其亲，里闬荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236860_comment'></div>友人邓肃志宏为榜其所居曰瑞花堂，且语之曰：物亦有不根而生者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236860_comment'></div>草木无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236860_comment'></div>造化之英不能自郁，其达而在上则有轮囷之云，扶疏之桂，行于天而现于月，若无俟乎根者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236860_comment'></div>其降而在人也，则所谓「将相公侯，宁有种乎」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236860_comment'></div>今超然以寒儒家连取文武二科，犹掇之也，异时将相盖唾手可取，较之卿云桂月，初不试根，若无甚异者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236860_comment'></div>然则瑞花之生，岂偶然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236860_comment'></div>虽然，闇者须明月乃烛之，旱者求苏云乃泽之，彼苍苍者岂徒为是无种之物以骇人哉，盖以种种而生者，政有赖于此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236860_comment'></div>超然其勉之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236860_comment'></div>吾辈所为将相云者，亦岂徒为观美而已乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236860_comment'></div>今天下须明求苏者，盖不可一二计，超然其勉之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236860_comment'></div>建炎三年七夕，邓肃序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1236860_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年8月4日</a>　八月，有跋文。作品：《跋朱乔年所跋王安石字》<div id='poem_1236871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋朱乔年所跋王安石字<span class='inlineComment2'>（建炎三年闰八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年8月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236871")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236871'>自荆舒祖桑弘羊以竭山海之利，故世无饱食之农；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236871_comment'></div>师秦商鞅以推不可行之法，故祖宗无可留之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236871_comment'></div>尊扬雄以赞《美新》之书，故学者甘为异姓之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236871_comment'></div>予读其书不能终篇，况学其字乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236871_comment'></div>朱乔年学道于西洛，学文于元祐，而能喜荆舒之文与其书如此，殆所谓恶而知其善者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236871_comment'></div>建炎三年闰月庚辰，栟榈老农。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1236871_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　有跋文。作品：《跋蔡君谟书》<div id='poem_1236873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋蔡君谟书</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236873")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236873'>观蔡襄之书，如读欧阳修之文，端严而不刻，温厚而不犯，太平之气郁然见于毫楮间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236873_comment'></div>当时朝廷之盛，盖可想而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236873_comment'></div>自崇宁以来，以文章字画为天下主盟者，较之仁庙之时，贤否如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236873_comment'></div>人才盛衰，信乎其可卜治乱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236873_comment'></div>事至今日，但可恸哭耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236873_comment'></div>建炎三年己酉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1236873_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　春，有诗王信州唱和。作品：《次韵王信州古风》《再次韵谢之二首》《第四章兼简其子》《次韵王信州游栖云》<div id='poem_76596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵王信州古风</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76596")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76596'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76596'>我昔少年日，气与风雷壮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76596'>一言既不合，掉头归望望。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76596'>誓将老烟霞，叩角耕闲旷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76596'>一日烦干旌，叩天舒孟浪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76596'>自譬舟一叶，沙溪春荡漾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76596'>百川傥已东，吾力那能障。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76596'>尚赖天地宽，未即崇山放。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76596'>栟榈付冷居，乃为世所长。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76596'>老妻画纸棋，赤脚沽村酿。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76596'>醉起舞彩衣，吾道颇休畅。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76596'>人杰又鼎来，不怕供诗帐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76596'>酬唱激清风，洗空烟雨瘴。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76596'>故人化鹤仙，穹庐共悽怆。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76596'>生还义更高，裹饭远相饷。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76596'>演山见长庚，醉眼不敢仰。<div id='poem_sentence_14_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_76596'>便结骑鲸游，不知飞燕谤。<div id='poem_sentence_15_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_76596'>兰亭最后来，德齿均所尚。<div id='poem_sentence_16_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_76596'>伤时虽慷慨，论事尤倜傥。<div id='poem_sentence_17_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_76596'>杯酒七峰下，逸思九天上。<div id='poem_sentence_18_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_76596'>万事俱可人，祇欠蛾眉唱。<div id='poem_sentence_19_76596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_76596'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_76596_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再次韵谢之<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76586")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76586'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76586'>四海王信州，志气老益壮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76586'>家学九夷闻，人物万夫望。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76586'>若使在庙堂，天下无怨旷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76586'>胡为一叶舟，也泛闽溪浪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76586'>顾余真断梗，江淮付摇漾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76586'>逢人辄倾倒，涉世无堤障。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76586'>既念越人瘠，仍欲郑声放。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76586'>斥下九天来，宜似幽怪长<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作幽怪多冗长）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76586'>邂逅忽相逢，琥珀倾新酿。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76586'>大<span class='inlineComment2'>（道光本作火）</span>急赓歌诗，胸臆赖舒畅。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76586'>我语无馀韵，日书甲乙帐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76586'>得君驱鳄手，不忧潮阳瘴。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76586'>三年去国心，海隅日悽怆。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76586'>东家久不燔，稚子将无饷。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76586'>诗成皆置之，万事吾不仰。<div id='poem_sentence_14_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_76586'>那复思重裘，区区欲止谤。<div id='poem_sentence_15_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_76586'>明朝更可人，芒鞋穷好尚。<div id='poem_sentence_16_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_76586'>遥知翠微中，高谈得纵傥。<div id='poem_sentence_17_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_76586'>至乐曲糵间，虚名钟鼎上。<div id='poem_sentence_18_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_76586'>轻重不须论，杯行且酬唱。<div id='poem_sentence_19_76586_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_76586'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_76586_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76585' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76585?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76585'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76585'>昌黎论佛骨，南行气亦<span class='inlineComment2'>（道光本作益）</span>壮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76585'>献书请镂玉，却起北归望。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76585'>香山最风流，诗酒事夷旷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76585'>那知闻琵琶，泪溅九江浪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76585'>此身苦海中，风波随荡漾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76585'>妄见分南北，无乃眼中障。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76585'>嗟我果何人，楚狂本天放。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76585'>外物不须论，有身今已长。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76585'>斥归水云乡，日醉莲花酿。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76585'>茗饮过陆羽，禅悦得文畅。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76585'>安此更何求，万里脱毡帐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76585'>死生则置之，北邙岂俱瘴。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76585'>使君怜我愚，了无逐客怆。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76585'>谓我耕白云，不独齐眉饷。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76585'>诗来觅欢处，光芒不可仰。<div id='poem_sentence_14_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_76585'>欲醉桃李春，那忧贝锦谤。<div id='poem_sentence_15_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_76585'>赤脚敢云无，社舞非时尚。<div id='poem_sentence_16_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_76585'>侯门列蛾眉，一见吾其傥。<div id='poem_sentence_17_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_76585'>抛砖此当先，积薪君在上。<div id='poem_sentence_18_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_76585'>更为李与苏，两家按新唱。<div id='poem_sentence_19_76585_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_76585'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_76585_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第四章兼简其子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年7月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76694")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76694'>虱卜虽萧条，虎筮固豪壮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76694'>要皆有得失，未息胸中望。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76694'>那知方寸地，太空等虚旷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76694'>川逝水不流，石高风自浪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76694'>郑五相府荣，谢三渔舟漾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76694'>穷达安在哉<span class='inlineComment2'>（曹抄作我）</span>，但瞒肉眼障。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76694'>鼓瑟铿尔舍，扶杖曝然放。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76694'>在我本不亏，底处更求长。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76694'>独挂百钱游，无人捉私酿。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76694'>醉归一腹春，满纸挥琴畅<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76694'>珍重江左王，德卲宜绛帐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76694'>天遣千里来，不顾闽山瘴。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76694'>人言臭味同，政可慰悽怆。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76694'>谁知金玉予，诗成即相饷。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76694'>笔力到天心，开卷人争仰。<div id='poem_sentence_14_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_76694'>但勿赋兔葵，小儿易生谤。<div id='poem_sentence_15_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_76694'>献之诗更奇，句法晋宋尚。<div id='poem_sentence_16_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_76694'>从渠得精深，嗟余真恍傥。<div id='poem_sentence_17_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_76694'>何当日相从，烦君更语上。<div id='poem_sentence_18_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_76694'>径追太古风，三叹聊十唱。<div id='poem_sentence_19_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_76694'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_76694'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_76694_0'>⑴ 自注：《风俗通》记凡琴曲和乐而作谓之畅，因忧愁而作谓之操。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_76694_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_76519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_76519'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76519'>胜游出林杪，参天仅一分。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76519_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76519'>从君如附骥，顾我愿为云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76519_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76519'>野色连空碧，幽香袭露薰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76519_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76519'>耦耕当卜此，横笛夜相闻<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《栟榈先生文集》卷一○）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76519_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76519'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76519_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　夏，又有诗王信州唱和。作品：《大水杂言》《次韵王信州》《再次韵》《次韵王信州三首》<div id='poem_76567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大水杂言</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76567")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76567'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76567'>前日雨如丝，缤纷杂朝雾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76567'>昨日雨如注，万壑争驰骛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76567'>今朝有霁色，作意在芒屦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76567'>那知复如倾，漫天飞瀑布。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76567'>介休借车振苍穹，十八叶幡如火红。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76567'>涛头起伏万银屋，河伯尽以山为宫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76567'>门前小艇疾飞鸿，挽我同趋急流中。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76567'>人生如梦贵适意，乘此可食千头龙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76567'>醉中举杯谢舟子，口腹自营吁可鄙。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76567'>不闻大禹不过门，血指为疏九年水。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76567'>何如乘风拜张坚<span class='inlineComment2'>（曹抄作转□照）</span>，唤取女娲来补天。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76567'>坐令赤子脱鱼腹，六合内外还桑田。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76567'>柳枝却下蛟龙约，谈笑支奇付铁索。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76567'>异时天上敢惊呼，斥作人间铛折脚。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76567'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_76567_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵王信州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76595")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76595'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76595'>煤炱飞上天，沉沉三日雾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76595'>银河一压摧，狂雨恣横骛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76595'>我恐铁骑来，疾驰不纳屦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76595'>气豪如项羽，势猛似黥布。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76595'>㳽漫江海接高穹，石牛未洗血泥红。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76595'>天吴八首真奇怪，咄嗟平地作银宫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76595'>我贫家火不星灶，赤脚灭没泥涂中。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76595'>目断晓风生少女，又复茅檐飞白龙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76595'>惭愧北来王夫子，籍籍声名满都鄙。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76595'>朝吟千赋暮千诗，松腴亦须枯海水。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76595'>莫倚文章似孟坚，未用风流追乐天。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76595'>且以光芒破阴晦，挽回日色到桑田。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76595'>乐岁天公有严约，斥落旄头沉贯索。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76595'>从公日醉三百杯，不怕西风动旗脚。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76595'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_76595_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76584?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_76584'>我闻张微子，仰天能服雾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76584'>又闻填海神，挥鞭石欲骛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76584'>二子呼不来，登山自纠屦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76584'>雷鼓速云阵，忽忽千岩布。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76584'>谁云九万隔高穹，玉女笑眼逼人红。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76584'>银浦遂倾瓜蔓水，雪浪欲浮天梁宫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76584'>孤孙得糟时哺翁，汎汎浮家烟浪中。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76584'>竞呼力士来西域，临江吹缩十丈龙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76584'>那知夏雨逢甲子，身如猪鸭不须鄙。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76584'>赤松作此岂无谋，门生主兵渠主水。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76584'>长江正欲截苻坚，夜亡智伯水如天。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76584'>此功朝成暮可霁，便当对月饮青田。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76584'>一雨从今十日约，要赓丰年入弦索。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76584'>凭君唤取阿戎俱，笑上天门同软脚。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76584_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76584'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_76584_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76518?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵王信州三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76518")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76518_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76518'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76518'>逐客难参国士忧，扶筇万里过闽瓯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76518'>藜羹充腹初无憾，楛矢踰江生计愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76518'>长夜漫漫不肯旦，梅霖灌灌未应休。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76518'>醉中我欲呼风伯，一扫阴霾霁九州。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76518'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76518_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76517?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76517'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76517'>风波未暇怨浮萍，多谢朋来慰此情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76517'>君似张凭真理窟，我惭侯喜得诗声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76517'>酒杯莫向吾徒浅，句法当<span class='inlineComment2'>（道光本作常）</span>令叔世惊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76517'>又恐诸公连茹去，堂堂王室要扶倾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76517_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76517'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76517_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76516?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76516_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76516'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76516'>平生耻为一身谋，枘凿方员两不投。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76516_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76516'>虮虱但知贪肉食，醯鸡何足语天游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76516_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76516'>雪馀自闭袁安户，月皎时登王粲楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76516_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76516'>更得吾人诗句好，当知此乐与天侔<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《栟榈先生文集》卷二）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76516_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76516'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76516_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　秋，又离家避难，有诗。作品：《别珠公诗》<div id='poem_76611' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76611' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76611?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别珠公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76611")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76611_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76611'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76611'>我顷诗成准敕恶，寒江夜度秋萧索。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76611'>曳杖从师得摩尼，洗空愁肠天地廓。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76611'>年来狂妄婴逆鳞，去国三秋又出奔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76611'>隔墙后得绨袍旧，一笑唤回逆旅春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76611'>我心不转嗟匪石，方壮两遭天上斥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76611'>处处逢君道价高，万指方袍趋法席。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76611'>白云天下妙林泉，看君又作新法缘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76611'>傥能容此无归客，便当结社追白莲。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76611_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76611'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_76611_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　与虞茂实交游唱和。作品：《谢虞守送酒》《别虞守》《原直》<div id='poem_76706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢虞守送酒</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76706")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76706'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76706'>瑟瑟严风鼓蓬户，对话春围两亡趣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76706'>使君送酒唤春来，坐使漫空翻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>柳絮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76706'>雪榭悬知雪未消，一目千里皆琼瑶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76706'>诗仙冷坐清入骨，便合九万抟扶摇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76706'>回首故园归未得，天意留人亦奇绝。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76706'>我今幸得贤主人，公亦未易有此客。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76706'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_76706'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_76706_0'>⑴ 道光本校：一作飞</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_76706_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_76612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别虞守</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76612")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76612'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76612'>闽山去天惟尺五，傍立怪石如蹲虎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76612'>点额龙墀万里归，未能赤脚走<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>风雨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76612'>惭愧使君肯相延，十日倾酒如流泉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76612'>文字兴馀亦不恶，红妆执乐艳神仙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76612'>明日冯驩出有车，远借仁风归故庐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76612'>不用回头重引领，行矣商霖到海隅。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76612'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_76612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_76612'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_76612_0'>⑴ 道光本校：一作追</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_76612_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1236884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236884?labeling=true' target='_blank'>原直</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236884")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236884_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236884'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236884'>世人尝谓穷达自天，余以谓穷达自人，非天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236884_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236884_comment'></div>伯夷饿，柳下惠黜，孟轲不用于战国之末，韩愈不得安其身于朝廷之上，比干剖心，子胥抉眼，真卿、杲卿碎其身于贼手：是为直必穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236884_comment'></div>子贡得驷马，苏秦得六印，宇文士及得安其职，张禹得全其身，崔日用得学士，宋之问得馆职，杨再思得宰相：是则为佞者必达矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236884_comment'></div>夫为直者必穷，为佞者必达，自古及今，莫不皆然，夫岂天哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236884_comment'></div>虽然，人生世上不过数十寒暑，盛衰得失，如蚁穴一梦耳，于此枉道丧节，以干妻孥之奉，一时沛然，自谓得志，殊不知万世之下使人闻其名而唾之，仅与禽兽比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236884_comment'></div>若正直之士，虽当时身不丝，腹不粟，斥窜流离，真若可怜者，然所谓浩然之气，历千百年犹与日月争光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236884_comment'></div>以此校彼，孰久孰近？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236884_comment'></div>故君子宁饿、宁黜、宁不用于世、宁不得安其身于朝廷之上，至于剖心抉眼，碎于贼手，亦宁任之，惟直不可变耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236884_comment'></div>余生踪迹几遍天下，求其不以穷达生死少变其直者，虽间有之，要不可以多得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236884_comment'></div>建炎初，余谪归沙邑，有主簿虞君茂实讳某者相遇，视其貌温而谨，听其言慎而信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236884_comment'></div>退窃自幸曰：「是必学者，非止为科举之士耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236884_comment'></div>予以得罪至重，流落益久，君又安于小官，不能遽去，忽忽相从且三年矣，视君所为，犹一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236884_comment'></div>与人无亲疏贵贱，一切以诚心待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236884_comment'></div>闻人有善，欣然若己有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236884_comment'></div>及论朋友之过，虽面颜发赤，勿顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236884_comment'></div>其事官长，亦不能少变辞色，作寸进计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236884_comment'></div>顾虽斋庖索然殆不能烟，青衫百结如霜后叶，其自处如得志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236884_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236884_comment'></div>君真坐直而穷者，君真不以穷而变其直者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236884_comment'></div>此余所以愿与交游之末，不敢以罪逐孤踪自为君弃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236884_comment'></div>孔子论三友，以友直为最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236884_comment'></div>佛氏论四友，以华友、秤友为可鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236884_comment'></div>盖华因时为盛衰，秤视物为低昂，此岂可与正直之友同日而语哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236884_comment'></div>君今别余而东矣，恐无规余失者，余于是黯然作恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236884_comment'></div>惜君之行也，作《原直》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1236884_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='1fa245539f1348ba9452b2bd76cbd68b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1fa245539f1348ba9452b2bd76cbd68b");'><span id='1fa245539f1348ba9452b2bd76cbd68b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>，41岁</div><div id='1fa245539f1348ba9452b2bd76cbd68b' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>初春，遇盗奉亲避乱，离沙县赴福唐，过黄杨岩，有诗。作品：《黄杨岩》<div id='poem_76696' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76696' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76696?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄杨岩<span class='inlineComment2'>（万历本题作同冯阳游黄杨岩）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76696")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76696'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76696'>石壁巉岩惊鬼划，异草幽花锁春色。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76696'>群山迤逦不能高，突兀独磨霄汉碧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76696'>芒鞋千尺上崔嵬，手摘星辰脚底雷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76696'>拨破烟云得洞户，醉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>眼恐是天门开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76696'>入门嵯峨森紫玉，冷风吹面天香馥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76696'>箕踞胡床<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>挥麈尾，万指未充空洞腹。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76696'>我因避地访名山，扁舟夜渡沙溪寒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76696'>辛勤博此一笑喜，太平犹在水云间。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76696'>猛将今无三角虎，狐狸昼号鳅鳝舞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76696'>灵岩知有老龙藏，挽出人间作霖雨。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76696'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_76696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_76696'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_76696_0'>⑴ 原字缺坏，据道光本、曹抄补</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_76696_0'>⑵ 箕、床二字原缺，据道光本、曹抄补</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_76696_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>举家外出避难，离沙县赴福唐，有诗。作品：《避贼引》<div id='poem_76723' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76723' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76723?labeling=true' target='_blank'>避贼引</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76723")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76723_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76723'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76723'>羽檄星驰暴客起，西望烽烟无百里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76723'>夜半惊呼得渔舠，老稚相携三百指。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76723'>蠖屈蛇盘破蓬底，忽欲骞身风刮耳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76723'>沙汀舣岸少依刘，万斛愁情空一洗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76723'>回思当年侍玉皇，禁垣夜直宫漏长。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76723'>驱驰谁谓遽如许，客枕不安云水乡。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76723'>前日蹇驴冲火烈，今此扁舟压残雪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76723'>隆暑祁寒欲少休，钲鼓迫人如地裂。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76723'>草庐安得无卧龙，奉天政赖陆宣公。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76723'>凭谁急呼人杰起，使我叩角歌尧风。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76723'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_76723_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>志宏作《避贼引》后，师皋和之，志宏又次其韵。作品：《次韵师皋》<div id='poem_76597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵师皋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76597")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76597'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76597'>平生论兵轻白起，端欲采芝追甪里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76597'>谁遣声名到人间，役役十年空血指。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76597'>天狗堕地嗟未已，雷声屡迫君王耳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76597'>闽山今复暗旌旗，四望长安泪如洗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76597'>羡君好古慕羲皇，品流不减刘真长。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76597'>舍我帡幪得甘寝，徬徨忽在无何乡。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76597'>安得大明如火烈，坐令鼠辈消春雪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76597'>六合内外还桑田，乾坤不容异姓裂。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76597'>看君躣马如游龙，醉中脱帽造王公。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76597'>高堂请志中兴事，吉甫作诵穆清风。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76597'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_76597_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>举家外出避难，离沙县赴福唐，有诗。作品：《避地山谷》<div id='poem_76721' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76721' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76721?labeling=true' target='_blank'>避地山谷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76721")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76721_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76721'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76721'>大禹不到处，石壁谁凿开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76721'>云端欲相搏，飞出白云来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76721'>馀沫乱飞雪，雄声敌春雷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76721'>溯流涌百尺，银山陟崔嵬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76721'>顾我虽逐客，解雨已春回。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76721'>嗟此天尽处，胡为乎来哉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76721'>萱堂有垂白，蓬室纷提孩。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76721'>内外三百指，奔窜若为怀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76721'>我疑云水间，亦有天下才。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76721'>何时日三锡，一振纪律颓。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76721'>羲和傥中天，六合无氛埃。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76721'>鼠壤与蚁穴，不风当自摧。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76721'>坐令陋巷中，依旧乐颜回。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76721'>亦能书夷狄，朝会叩天阶。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76721_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76721'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_76721_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>奉亲避乱，离沙县赴福唐，过雷霹雳滩，有诗。作品：《避地过雷霹雳滩》<div id='poem_76722' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76722' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76722?labeling=true' target='_blank'>避地过雷霹滩<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76722")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_76722_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_76722_0'>① 诗集题作过雷霹雳滩，明嘉靖《延平府志》卷二○题作雷霹雳滩</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76722'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76722'>门前又见马如流，兵革缤纷几日休。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76722'>岭似车盘方税驾，滩如雷霹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>更行舟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76722'>豺狼敢侮乾坤大，江海徒深虮虱忧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76722'>安得将坛登李郭，挽回羲御<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>照神州。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76722'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_76722'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_76722_0'>⑴ 诗集作霹雳、道光本作雷劈</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_76722_0'>⑵ 诗集、《延平府志》作驭</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_76722_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>奉亲避乱，离沙县赴福唐，过龙兴寺，有诗。作品：《龙兴避难》<div id='poem_76582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76582?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龙兴避难</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76582")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76582'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76582'>傍山怪石如蹲虎，绝顶去天无尺五。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76582'>却披丛棘下山腰，丹碧照空飞栋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>宇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76582'>道人养道<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗集作蓬户）</span>厌尘劳，避世只嫌山不高。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76582'>那知行空老曼倩，窃食不遗<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗集作当年）</span>王母桃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76582'>松桧参天门昼闭，碧玉撷蔬饭炊雪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76582'>百年冷坐无车音，一旦偕来真恶客。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76582'>当知喧寂无殊观，出世何妨在世间。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76582'>能致吾人师作古，龙兴今日始开山。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76582'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_76582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_76582'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_76582_0'>⑴ 道光本校：丹碧一作晶荧，栋一作绀</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_76582_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

id='poem_title_76616_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76616'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76616'>安得守令体宸衷，不复区区踵前踪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76616'>但为君王安百姓，圃中无日不春<span class='inlineComment2'>（道光本作东）</span>风<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76616'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_76616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_76616'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_76616_1'>⑴ 诗集作天地一圃乐何穷。按：此十一章诗前，原附有《进花石诗状》，今移置此：太学生臣郑肃。右臣窃见东南所进花木怪石无甚异者，又不能无费。臣今有策，欲取天下奇绝之观，毕置皇帝陛下圃中。比之今日所贡者，固万万胜之，较之今日之费，则无万分之一。臣已撰成文字一轴，伏望宣索。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_76616_comment'></div></div><br <div class='label1' id='1adb671dcfa145d7b07c833bd31a5c96_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1adb671dcfa145d7b07c833bd31a5c96");'><span id='1adb671dcfa145d7b07c833bd31a5c96_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>，32岁</div><div id='1adb671dcfa145d7b07c833bd31a5c96' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年6月</a>　上庐山，有诗。作品：《庐山》<div id='poem_76613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76613")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76613'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76613'>平生作意庐山游，往来却贪吴越舟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76613'>陛下许臣鞭匹马，芒鞋因得款清幽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76613'>是时六月蒸炎暑，六合黄尘空一雨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76613'>上方冷翠袭衣襟，便觉笑谈在天宇<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《栟榈先生文集》卷五）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76613'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_76613_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
南平（剑浦）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3a3dab09dda343e29a66a27951221d7e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3a3dab09dda343e29a66a27951221d7e");'><span id='3a3dab09dda343e29a66a27951221d7e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>，33岁</div><div id='3a3dab09dda343e29a66a27951221d7e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年8月5日</a>　游南平，作《题开平院》<div id='poem_1236901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236901?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题开平院</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和五年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236901")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236901'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236901'>栟榈邓某志宏游此，胜景超然，固非尘俗鄙，而住持材成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236901_comment'></div>新诗健笔，气欲凌云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236901_comment'></div>清谈终日，了不及世事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236901_comment'></div>白莲结社，当在异日，率俗而行，惘然作恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236901_comment'></div>宣和癸卯八月五日志之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1236901_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

id='poem_sentence_11_76672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76672'>老谋大节数子并，行见犁庭灭金虏。<div id='poem_sentence_12_76672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_76672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_76672'>规模共佐李西平，庙貌不移旧钟簴。<div id='poem_sentence_15_76672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/1236847?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上李右丞相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年6月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1236847'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236847'>伏审光被殊恩，擢参大政，士民交庆，社稷增辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236847_comment'></div>恭惟右丞相公先生道贯天人，气弥寰宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236847_comment'></div>尽忠于社稷，遑恤其妻孥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236847_comment'></div>初擢柏台，尝斥脱靴之力士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236847_comment'></div>继亲香案，遂同折槛之朱云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236847_comment'></div>扁舟既落于穷山，尺纸不干于要路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236847_comment'></div>惟居穷固，略无希进之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236847_comment'></div>故位崇高，不为患失之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236847_comment'></div>敢陈大计，默契宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236847_comment'></div>洗空天上之旄头，拥出云端之北极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236847_comment'></div>措九州于磐石，脱万姓于虎牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236847_comment'></div>拨乱殊勋，既出子房之帷幄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236847_comment'></div>守成有道，更资傅说之盐梅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236847_comment'></div>谷腹丝身，要观实效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236847_comment'></div>泥金检玉，何取虚文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236847_comment'></div>某顷以青衿，久从绛帐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236847_comment'></div>兀居闽岭，但足一泓之牛蹄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236847_comment'></div>坐想沙堤，上抟万里之羊角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236847_comment'></div>虽乏攀鳞之业，幸为击壤之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236847_comment'></div>其欣愉者，实倍伦等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1236847_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年6月6日</a>　上札子论周武仲，朝廷以所言非实，不听。作品：《第十二札子》<br /><a id='poem_content_76694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76694'>虱卜虽萧条，虎筮固豪壮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76694'>在我本不亏，底处更求长。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_76694'>谁知金玉予，诗成即相饷。<div id='poem_sentence_13_76694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 光泽

-----title
玉山

<div class='label1' id='be82e5c2f3814a389e54dc239cb5ead2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("be82e5c2f3814a389e54dc239cb5ead2");'><span id='be82e5c2f3814a389e54dc239cb5ead2_link' id='poem_sentence_4_76581'>今年十月间，叛卒起南方。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76581'>官兵且二万，一旦忽已亡。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76581'>一身幸无责，奉亲走穷荒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_76581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_76581'>那知奔窜中，一乐得未尝。<div id='poem_sentence_18_76581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_76581_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_76502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76502?labeling=true' 松溪
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='50a918b6af6f4a0b8adff11c680c3a68_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("50a918b6af6f4a0b8adff11c680c3a68");'><span id='50a918b6af6f4a0b8adff11c680c3a68_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，40岁</div><div id='50a918b6af6f4a0b8adff11c680c3a68' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年12月10日</a>　在杉口，作《跋了翁墨迹》<div id='poem_1236863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题了翁墨迹</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236863")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236863'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236863'>颜鲁公忠义之气充塞宇宙，故散落毫楮间者，皆铜筋铁骨，使人望之凛然，不寒而慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236863_comment'></div>顾其规规从事墨池笔冢，而至于斯乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236863_comment'></div>观了翁作字，便知其与鲁公同科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236863_comment'></div>盖其胸中所蕴有默契者，亦非可以间架求也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236863_comment'></div>梦得宝此，岂偶然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236863_comment'></div>建炎四年十二月初十日，邓某书于杉口。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1236863_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
福州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6b71d85441ca49bcb7cc983698bc1452_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6b71d85441ca49bcb7cc983698bc1452");'><span id='6b71d85441ca49bcb7cc983698bc1452_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1132')">1131-1132年</a>，41-42岁</div><div id='6b71d85441ca49bcb7cc983698bc1452' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年4月</a>　志宏读李纲诗后，作跋。作品：《跋李丞相赠邓成材判官诗》<div id='poem_1236874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋李丞相赠邓成材判官诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236874")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236874'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236874'>建炎三年冬十一月，金寇破洪，传檄下建昌，当时无敢谁何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236874_comment'></div>判官邓柞独不可，曰：「宁死耳，忍负吾君父乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236874_comment'></div>拂袖而去，誓不降辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236874_comment'></div>南奔闽山，斥还仆御，脱身万死，而臣子之节立矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236874_comment'></div>大丞相李公闻而壮之，因邓有诗，遂次其韵，既赞其所已至，又勉其所当为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236874_comment'></div>锵金戛玉，铿然廊庙之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236874_comment'></div>盖道德之妙形于言咏，非止以句法高天下耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236874_comment'></div>邓子之学，其光矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236874_comment'></div>宣和间，邓子尝以诸生从公游于沙阳，得其议论之馀，遂能所立如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236874_comment'></div>今公相期益厚，又非前日比，他时设施当如何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236874_comment'></div>因读公诗，谨题其后，盖非特勉子耳，亦自警云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236874_comment'></div>时绍兴元年四月晦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1236874_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　与邓成材唱和。作品：《和邓成材五绝》《送成材》<div id='poem_76487' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76487' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76487?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和邓成材五绝<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76487")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_76487_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76487'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76487'>扶筇欲过北山来，政赖诗囊一笑开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76487'>故走溪山寻胜景，为君携向笔端来<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76487'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_76487_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_76487'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_76487_0'>⑴ 自注：仆在杉口，未谒成材，先游灵岩。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_76487_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_76484' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76484' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_1236879_comment'></div>至宣和间，边隙一开，海内鼎沸，二圣播迁，远在沙漠，而天下横尸当以亿兆计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236879_comment'></div>然后知前辈爱主忧民之心，为天下后世之虑；<div class='inline' class='authorDate'>（1132年3月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236900")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236900'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236900'>莆田陈汝作邀三山黄尧翁、毗陵张泰定、延平邓志宏晚集贤沙寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236900_comment'></div>宿雨初霁，景物一新，遂获纵观飞山之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236900_comment'></div>岂衡山之云，特为退之一开乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236900_comment'></div>佥曰：当志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236900_comment'></div>绍兴二年三月丙午。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1236900_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月6日</a>　李纲始率师离福州，志宏作诗相送。作品：《送李丞相四路宣抚》<div id='poem_76678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_76678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/76678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李丞相四路宣抚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_76678")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_76678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_76678'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_76678'>冷风吹海烟雾开，绣衣使者天上来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_76678'>手持天书传天语，促起天下豪杰魁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_76678'>下堂拜命汗如雨，上堂鸣鼓旌旄举。<div id='poem_sentence_2_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_76678'>要令南国生清风，不辞马上蒸溽暑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_76678'>平生直气高苍穹，四海草木闻威风。<div id='poem_sentence_4_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_76678'>业以自任如伊尹，那使流言动周公。<div id='poem_sentence_5_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_76678'>君臣今日机锋契，六十九州归重寄。<div id='poem_sentence_6_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_76678'>屠龙事业警狗偷，谈笑定缚吴元济。<div id='poem_sentence_7_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_76678'>功成上天相都俞，指呼瓦皪化华胥。<div id='poem_sentence_8_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_76678'>日辟农桑三万里，二十四考书中书。<div id='poem_sentence_9_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_76678'>我今流落穷吞纸，蟾蜍爬沙鞭不起。<div id='poem_sentence_10_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_76678'>归欤自筑茅三间，为作野史书雄伟。<div id='poem_sentence_11_76678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_76678'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_76678_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月</a>　曾致书李易言生活近况。作品：《与李状元工部》<div id='poem_1236844' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236844' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236844?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李状元工部书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(33058, "宋", "邓肃", "poem_title_1236844")'>邓肃</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236844_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236844'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236844'>某顿首再拜顺之工部状元老兄：自罗源人去，匆匆具状，并以恶语呈浼，想无不达者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236844_comment'></div>即日溽暑，伏惟台候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236844_comment'></div>某客此馀年，巢南之念，无食顷置，但以乡里残破之后，斗米千钱，鸡豚蔬笋一切无有，疫疠大作，死亡相枕，遂不能即去，且复须止耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236844_comment'></div>但不知仰俯三百，指意将安归乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236844_comment'></div>水到渠成之语，东坡其欺我哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236844_comment'></div>虽然，穷中之味，非吾辈不能堪，非处之久不能知其味之永也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236844_comment'></div>顷在都城，陷身虏帐，幸而脱归，又落风波之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236844_comment'></div>列士枭首，时无不免，赖圣主赦于必死，遂获南归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236844_comment'></div>方安畎亩，为终焉计，又为寇盗所迫，来客海嵎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236844_comment'></div>今虽困卧流离，岂不愈于前日九死之地乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236844_comment'></div>以此亦能自安，幸老兄毋重为小人念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236844_comment'></div>老兄湖南之行，竟可免否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236844_comment'></div>兰省亦岂能久留老兄耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236844_comment'></div>官无大小，要行其志，志不可行，则袖手旁观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236844_comment'></div>一时士君子进退出处之节，弥纶献替之道，与夫谈笑议论之馀，其善者固可师，而不然者亦可戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236844_comment'></div>此杖藜观物化、亦以观我生之义也，岂不愈于纸上之学乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236844_comment'></div>顺之学富识高，追配古人，固无事此，然舍此亦无以寓吾志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236844_comment'></div>盖所谓「优哉游哉，聊以卒岁」耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236844_comment'></div>丞公数相过否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236844_comment'></div>辄以数字浼之，议论狂直，殊愧犯分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236844_comment'></div>然吾徒所以相好，政在阿堵之中，知我罪我，俱在《春秋》乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236844_comment'></div>贯道早晚如闽中，想遂相从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236844_comment'></div>子安失意，将不安此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236844_comment'></div>德和将罢新任，文明亦以替去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236844_comment'></div>回首前日凤池之游，岂非梦耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236844_comment'></div>然人生孰非梦，聚散无常，即生灭法于此，思之则生灭俱灭，又何足计乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236844_comment'></div>欲言无穷，恨不能多幅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236844_comment'></div>何日握手一笑，以写此心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236844_comment'></div>临纸东瞻，精爽俱遗，更冀惠序加爱，以寿君亲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1236844_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　上章乞致仕。转承事郎致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月9日</a>　五月初九，病卒。<br /></div>
